vīryavānd caturthaḥ kīcakas teṣāṃ pañcamaṃ nānuśuśrumaḥd anyonyānantarabalāḥ parasparajayaiṣiṇaḥd bāhuyuddham abhīpsanto nityaṃ saṃrabdhamānasāḥd tenāham avagacchāmi pratyayena vṛkodaramd manasy abhiniviṣṭaṃ me vyaktaṃ jīvanti pāṇḍavāḥd tatrāhaṃ kīcakaṃ manye bhīmasenena māritamd sairandhrīṃ draupadīṃ manye nātra kāryā vicāraṇād śaṅke kṛṣṇānimittaṃ tu bhīmasenena kīcakaḥd gandharvavyapadeśena hato niśi mahābalaḥd ko hi śakto paro bhīmāt kīcakaṃ hantum ojasād śastraṃ vinā bāhuvīryāt tathā sarvāṅgacūrṇitamd mardituṃ vā tathā śīghraṃ carmamāṃsāsthicūrṇitamd rūpam anyat samāsthāya bhīmasyaitad viceṣṭitamd dhruvaṃ kṛṣṇānimittaṃ tu bhīmasenena sūtajaḥd gandharvavyapadeśena hato niśi na saṃśayaḥd pitāmahena ye coktā deśasya ca janasya cad guṇās te matsyarāṣṭreṣu bahuśo pi mayā śrutāḥd virāṭanagare manye pāṇḍavāś channacāriṇaḥd nivasanti pure ramye tatra yātrā vidhīyatāmd matsyarāṣṭraṃ gamiṣyāmo grahīṣyāmaś ca godhanamd gṛhīte godhane nūnaṃ te pi yotsyanti pāṇḍavāḥd apūrṇe samaye cāpi yadi paśyāma pāṇḍavānd dvādaśānyāni varṣāṇi pravekṣyanti punar vanamd tasmād anyatareṇāpi lābho smākaṃ bhaviṣyatid kośavṛddhir ihāsmākaṃ śatrūṇāṃ nidhanaṃ bhavetd kathaṃ suyodhanaṃ gacched yudhiṣṭhirabhṛtaḥ purād etac cāpi vadaty eṣa mātsyaḥ paribhavān mayid tasmāt kartavyam etad vai tasmin yātrā vidhīyatāmd etat sunītaṃ manye haṃ sarveṣāṃ yadi rocate vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa atha rājā trigartānāṃ suśarmā rathayūthapaḥb pūrvam ābhāṣya karṇena tathā duḥśāsanena cac prāptakālam idaṃ vākyam uvāca tvarito bhṛśama asakṛn nikṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ matsyaiḥ sālveyakaiḥ sahac sūtena caiva matsyasya kīcakena punaḥ punaḥa bādhito bandhubhiḥ sārdhaṃ balād balavatā vibhoc sa karṇam abhyudīkṣyātha duryodhanam abhāṣataa asakṛn matsyarājñā me rāṣṭraṃ bādhitam ojasāc praṇetā kīcakaś cāsya balavān abhavat purāa krūro marṣī sa duṣṭātmā bhuvi prakhyātavikramaḥc nihatas tatra gandharvaiḥ pāpakarmā nṛśaṃsavāna tasmiṃś ca nihate rājan hīnadarpo nirāśrayaḥc bhaviṣyati nirutsāho virāṭa iti me matiḥa tatra yātrā mama matā yadi te rocate naghac kauravāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ karṇasya ca mahātmanaḥa etat prāptam ahaṃ manye kāryam ātyayikaṃ hitamc rāṣṭraṃ tasyābhiyātv āśu bahudhānyasamākulama ādadāmo sya ratnāni vividhāni vasūni cac grāmān rāṣṭrāṇi vā tasya hariṣyāmo vibhāgaśaḥa atha vā gosahasrāṇi bahūni ca śubhāni cab vidhamitvā hariṣyāmaḥ praviśya ca purād balamc vividhāni hariṣyāmaḥ pratipīḍya puraṃ balāta kauravaiḥ saha saṃgamya trigartaiś ca viśāṃ patec gās tasyāpaharāmāśu saha sarvaiḥ susaṃhatāḥa saṃdhiṃ vā tena kṛtvā tu nibadhnīmo sya pauruṣamc hatvā cāsya camūṃ kṛtsnāṃ vaśam anvānayāmahea taṃ vaśe nyāyataḥ kṛtvā sukhaṃ vatsyāmahe vayamc bhavato balavṛddhiś ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥa tac chrutvā vacanaṃ tasya karṇo rājānam abravītc sūktaṃ suśarmaṇā vākyaṃ prāptakālaṃ hitaṃ ca naḥa tasmāt kṣipraṃ viniryāmo yojayitvā varūthinīmb yady etat te bhirucitaṃ mama caitad dhi rocatec vibhajya cāpy anīkāni yathā vā manyase naghaa prajñāvān kuruvṛddho yaṃ sarveṣāṃ naḥ pitāmahaḥc ācāryaś ca tathā droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvatas tathāa manyante te yathā sarve tathā yātrā vidhīyatāmc saṃmantrya cāśu gacchāmaḥ sādhanārthaṃ mahīpateḥa kiṃ ca naḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ kāryaṃ hīnārthabalapauruṣaiḥc atyarthaṃ vā pranaṣṭās te prāptā vāpi yamakṣayamd tad bhavāṃś caturaṅgeṇa balena mahatā vṛtaḥa yāmo rājann anudvignā virāṭaviṣayaṃ vayamc ādāsyāmo hi gās tasya vividhāni vasūni cad duryodhana uvācad uktam etad vidheyaṃ vā vākyam uktaṃ tvayānaghad yadaiva cāraiḥ prahitair ihāgamya niveditamd nidhanaṃ sūtaputrasya kīcakasya balīyasaḥd tadaiva hi mahācintā hṛdi pāṇḍusutān pratid kīcakaṃ balasaṃpannaṃ nānyo hantā vṛkodarātd nityam eva hi pārthānāṃ virāṭaḥ priyam icchatid tasmiṃs te cāpi viśvastā nivāsāya sthitā dhruvamd pitāmahena yac coktaṃ cihnaṃ pārthābhivedaned tad dhi rājño virāṭasya śrūyate viṣaye kilad tat tatra gatvā karṇāśu virāṭaṃ godhanaṃ vayamd gṛhṇīmas tasya rāṣṭraṃ ca pramathya svabalair yutāḥd anuyāsyanti te cāsmān virāṭasya hitaiṣiṇaḥd tatra vetsyāmahe tān vai buddhvā caiṣāṃ yathāgatimd apūrṇasamayān bhūyo vanāya gamayāmahed hatvāpi caitāṃs tatraiva sukhaṃ bhokṣyāma medinīmd alpāvaśiṣṭaḥ kālo yaṃ samayaś ca vibhāti med udyojayāma sainyāni śvobhūte gamanaṃ pratid karṇa uvācad yadi tatra sma te pārthā bhaveyū rājasattamad siddhiṃ cobhayakīṃ tat syāt tathāpi khalu yāsyathad nigrahād yā virāṭasya pāṇḍavānāṃ prabodhanamd dīnās te kośahīnāś ca vanavāsena karśitāḥd sukhena hantum arhanti atha pravrājanāya vaia tato duryodhano rājā vākyam ādāya tasya tatc vaikartanasya karṇasya kṣipram ājñāpayat svayama śāsane nityasaṃyuktaṃ duḥśāsanam anantaramc saha vṛddhais tu saṃmantrya kṣipraṃ yojaya vāhinīma yathoddeśaṃ ca gacchāmaḥ sahitāḥ sarvakauravaiḥc suśarmā tu yathoddiṣṭaṃ deśaṃ yātu mahārathaḥa trigartaiḥ sahito rājā samagrabalavāhanaḥc prāg eva hi susaṃvīto matsyasya viṣayaṃ pratia jaghanyato vayaṃ tatra yāsyāmo divasāntaramc viṣayaṃ matsyarājasya susamṛddhaṃ susaṃhatāḥd suśarmaṇā gṛhīte tu matsyarājasya godhaned virāṭaḥ sainyam ādāya trigartaiḥ saha yotsyated aparaṃ divasaṃ gās tu tatra gṛhṇantu kauravāḥd gavārthe pāṇḍavās tatra yotsyanti kurubhiḥ sahaa te yātvā sahasā tatra virāṭanagaraṃ pratic kṣipraṃ gopān samāsādya gṛhṇantu vipulaṃ dhanama gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi śrīmanti guṇavanti cac vayam api nigṛhṇīmo dvidhā kṛtvā varūthinīm asatāṃ saṅgadoṣeṇa sādhavo yānti vikriyām duryodhanaprasaṅgena bhīṣmo gograhaṇe gataḥ saṃnaddhā rathinaḥ sarve sapadātibalotkaṭāḥ prativairaṃ cikīrṣanto goṣu saṃnyapatan parea sa sma gatvā yathoddiṣṭāṃ diśaṃ vahner mahīpatiḥc ādatta gāḥ suśarmātha gharmapakṣasya saptamīma aparaṃ divasaṃ sarve rājan saṃbhūya kauravāḥc aṣṭamyāṃ tāny agṛhṇanta gokulāni sahasraśaḥd kauravās tu mahāvīryā matsyānāṃ viṣayāntare vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tatas teṣāṃ mahārāja tatraivāmitatejasāmc chadmaliṅgapraviṣṭānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāma vyatītaḥ samayaḥ samyag vasatāṃ vai purottamec kurvatāṃ tasya karmāṇi virāṭasya mahīpateḥd kīcake tu hate rājā virāṭaḥ paravīrahād āsāṃ cakre sahāmātyaḥ kuntīputraś ca vīryavāna tatas trayodaśasyānte tasya varṣasya bhāratac suśarmaṇā gṛhītaṃ tu godhanaṃ tarasā bahud tataḥ śabdo mahān āsīd reṇuś ca divam aspṛśatd śaṅkhadundubhinirghoṣo bherīṇāṃ ca mahāsvanaḥd gavāśvarathanāgānāṃ narāṇāṃ ca padātināmd evaṃ tais tv abhiniryāya matsyarājasya godhaned trigartair gṛhyamāṇe tu gopālāḥ pratyaṣedhayand atha trigartā bahavaḥ parigṛhya dhanaṃ bahud parikṣipya hayaiḥ śīghrai rathavrātaiś ca bhāratad gopālān pratyayudhyanta raṇe kṛtvā jaye dhṛtimd te hanyamānā bahubhiḥ prāsatomarapāṇibhiḥd gopālā gokule bhaktā vārayām āsur ojasād paraśvadhaiś ca musalair bhiṇḍipālaiś ca mudgaraiḥd gopālāḥ karpaṇaiś citrair jaghnur aśvān samantataḥd te hanyamānāḥ saṃkruddhās trigartā rathayodhinaḥd visṛjya śaravarṣāṇi gopān vyadrāvayan raṇed tato yuvānaḥ saṃbhītāḥ śvasanto reṇuguṇṭhitāḥa tato javena mahatā gopāḥ puram athāvrajatc apaśyan matsyarājaṃ ca rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalīd virāṭanagaraṃ prāpya narā rājānam abruvana śūraiḥ parivṛtaṃ yodhaiḥ kuṇḍalāṅgadadhāribhiḥc sadbhiś ca mantribhiḥ sārdhaṃ pāṇḍavaiś ca nararṣabhaiḥa taṃ sabhāyāṃ mahārājam āsīnaṃ rāṣṭravardhanamc so bravīd upasaṃgamya virāṭaṃ praṇatas tadāa asmān yudhi vinirjitya paribhūya sabāndhavānc gavāṃ śatasahasrāṇi trigartāḥ kālayanti tee tān parīpsa manuṣyendra mā neśuḥ paśavas tavaf vaiśaṃpāyanaḥf śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ gopālānām ariṃdamaḥa tac chrutvā nṛpatiḥ senāṃ matsyānāṃ samayojayatc rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pattidhvajasamākulāmd samādiśya tadā rājā matsyānāṃ paravīrahāa rājāno rājaputrāś ca tanutrāṇy atra bhejirec bhānumanti vicitrāṇi sūpasevyāni bhāgaśaḥd pṛthak kāñcanasaṃnāhān ratheṣv aśvān ayojayand utkṛṣya pāśān maurvīṇāṃ vīrāś cāpeṣv ayojayana savajrāyasagarbhaṃ tu kavacaṃ taptakāñcanamc virāṭasya priyo bhrātā śatānīko bhyahārayata sarvapārasavaṃ varma kalyāṇapaṭalaṃ dṛḍhamc śatānīkād avarajo madirāśvo bhyahārayata śatasūryaṃ śatāvartaṃ śatabindu śatākṣimatc abhedyakalpaṃ matsyānāṃ rājā kavacam āharata utsedhe yasya padmāni śataṃ saugandhikāni cac suvarṇapṛṣṭhaṃ sūryābhaṃ sūryadatto bhyahārayata dṛḍham āyasagarbhaṃ tu śvetaṃ varma śatākṣimatc virāṭasya suto jyeṣṭho vīraḥ śaṅkho bhyahārayata śataśaś ca tanutrāṇi yathāsvāni mahārathāḥc yotsyamānābhyanahyanta devarūpāḥ prahāriṇaḥa sūpaskareṣu śubhreṣu mahatsu ca mahārathāḥc pṛthak kāñcanasaṃnāhān ratheṣv aśvān ayojayana sūryacandrapratīkāśo rathe divye hiraṇmayaḥc mahānubhāvo matsyasya dhvaja ucchiśriye tadāa athānyān vividhākārān dhvajān hemavibhūṣitānb vājino vividhāṃś caiva taptakāñcanabhūṣaṇānc yathāsvaṃ kṣatriyāḥ śūrā ratheṣu samayojayand ratheṣu yujyamāneṣu kaṅko rājānam abravītd mayāpy astraṃ caturmārgam avāptam ṛṣisattamātd daṃśito ratham āsthāya padaṃ niryāmy ahaṃ gavāmd ayaṃ ca balavāñ chūro valalo dṛśyate naghad gosaṃkhyam aśvabandhaṃ ca ratheṣu samayojayad naite na jātu yudhyeyur gavārtham iti me matiḥa atha matsyo bravīd rājā śatānīkaṃ jaghanyajamc kaṅkaballavagopālā dāmagranthiś ca vīryavānd tantipālaś ca gosaṃkhyo ya etat puruṣarṣabhāḥe yudhyeyur iti me buddhir vartate nātra saṃśayaḥa eteṣām api dīyantāṃ rathā dhvajapatākinaḥc kavacāni vicitrāṇi dṛḍhāni ca mṛdūni cae pratimuñcantu gātreṣu dīyantām āyudhāni caa vīrāṅgarūpāḥ puruṣā nāgarājakaropamāḥc neme jātu na yudhyerann iti me dhīyate matiḥa etac chrutvā tu nṛpater vākyaṃ tvaritamānasaḥc śatānīkas tu pārthebhyo rathān rājan samādiśate sahadevāya rājñe ca bhīmāya nakulāya caa tān prahṛṣṭās tataḥ sūtā rājabhaktipuraskṛtāḥc nirdiṣṭān naradevena rathāñ śīghram ayojayana kavacāni vicitrāṇi dṛḍhāni ca mṛdūni cac virāṭaḥ prādiśad yāni teṣām akliṣṭakarmaṇāmd tāni te pratigṛhyāśu samanahyanta pāṇḍavāḥd vīrāś ca siṃhavikrāntā balavanto manasvinaḥe tāny āmucya śarīreṣu daṃśitās te paraṃtapāḥf rathān hayaiḥ susaṃpannān āsthāya ca narottamāḥf niryuyur muditāḥ pārthāḥ śatrusaṃghāvamardinaḥa tarasvinaś channarūpāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥb rathān hemaparicchinnān āsthāya ca mahārathāḥb pāṇḍavā niryayur hṛṣṭā daṃśitā rājasattamāḥc virāṭam anvayuḥ paścāt sahitāḥ kurupuṃgavāḥe catvāro bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ satyavikramāḥf dīrghāṇāṃ ca dṛḍhānāṃ ca dhanuṣāṃ te yathābalamf utkṛṣya pāśān maurvīṇāṃ vīrāś cāpeṣv ayojayanf tataḥ suvāsasaḥ sarve te vīrāś candanokṣitāḥf coditā naradevena kṣipram aśvān acodayanf te hayā hemasaṃchannā bṛhantaḥ sādhuvāhinaḥf coditāḥ pratyadṛśyanta pakṣiṇām iva paṅktayaḥa bhīmāś ca mattamātaṅgāḥ prabhinnakaraṭāmukhāḥc kṣaranta iva jīmūtāḥ sudantāḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanāḥa svārūḍhā yuddhakuśalaiḥ śikṣitair hastisādibhiḥc rājānam anvayuḥ paścāc calanta iva parvatāḥa viśāradānāṃ vaśyānāṃ hṛṣṭānāṃ cānuyāyināmb viṃśatis tu sahasrāṇi narāṇām anuyāyināmc aṣṭau rathasahasrāṇi daśa nāgaśatāni cae ṣaṣṭiś cāśvasahasrāṇi matsyānām abhiniryayuḥf pūrṇe śatasahasre dve padātīnāṃ ca bhārataf etad balam aparyantaṃ matsyānām abhiniryayaua tad anīkaṃ virāṭasya śuśubhe bharatarṣabhab vasante bahupuṣpāḍhyaṃ kānanaṃ citritaṃ yathāc saṃprayātaṃ mahārāja ninīṣantaṃ gavāṃ padama tad balāgryaṃ virāṭasya saṃprasthitam aśobhatac dṛḍhāyudhajanākīrṇaṃ gajāśvarathasaṃkulam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa niryāya nagarāc chūrā vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥc trigartān aspṛśan matsyāḥ sūrye pariṇate satida trigartā aspṛśan mātsyān pūrvam eva mahārathāḥa te trigartāś ca matsyāś ca saṃrabdhā yuddhadurmadāḥc anyonyam abhigarjanto goṣu gṛddhā mahābalāḥa bhīmāś ca mattamātaṅgās tomarāṅkuśacoditāḥc grāmaṇīyaiḥ samārūḍhāḥ kuśalair hastisādibhiḥa teṣāṃ samāgamo ghoras tumulo lomaharṣaṇaḥb ghnatāṃ parasparaṃ ghoro yamarāṣṭravivardhanaḥc devāsurasamo rājann āsīt sūrye vilambatid padātirathanāgendrahayārohabalaughavānd anyonyam abhyāpatatāṃ nighnatāṃ cetaretarama udatiṣṭhad rajo bhaumaṃ na prajñāyata kiṃ canac pakṣiṇaś cāpatan bhūmau sainyena rajasāvṛtāḥa iṣubhir vyatisaṃyadbhir ādityo ntaradhīyatac khadyotair iva saṃyuktam antarikṣaṃ vyarājatad rukmapuṅkhaiḥ sutīkṣṇāgrair vajrāgnisadṛśaprabhaiḥa rukmapṛṣṭhāni cāpāni vyatiṣaktāni dhanvināmc patatāṃ lokavīrāṇāṃ savyadakṣiṇam asyatāma rathā rathaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātaiś ca padātayaḥc sādibhiḥ sādinaś caiva gajaiś cāpi mahāgajāḥd rathinaḥ sādinaś cātra saṃprahāram akurvataa asibhiḥ paṭṭiśaiḥ prāsaiḥ śaktibhis tomarair apic saṃrabdhāḥ samare rājan nijaghnur itaretaramd antarikṣe gatir yeṣāṃ dadṛśuś cāpi vadhyatāma nighnantaḥ samare nyonyaṃ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥc na śekur abhisaṃrabdhāḥ śūrān kartuṃ parāṅmukhāna kḷptottaroṣṭhaṃ sunasaṃ kḷptakeśam alaṃkṛtamc adṛśyata śiraś chinnaṃ rajodhvastaṃ sakuṇḍalama adṛśyaṃs tatra gātrāṇi śaraiś chinnāni bhāgaśaḥc śālaskandhanikāśāni kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahāmṛdhea nāgabhoganikāśaiś ca bāhubhiś candanokṣitaiḥc ākīrṇā vasudhā tatra śirobhiś ca sakuṇḍalaiḥd rathināṃ rathibhiś cātra saṃprahāro bhyavartatad sādibhiḥ sādināṃ cātra pādātānāṃ padātibhiḥd yathā vā vāsasī ślakṣṇe mahārajatarañjited bibhratī yuvatī śyāmā bhāti tadvad vasuṃdharāa upaśāmyad rajo bhaumaṃ rudhireṇa prasarpatāc kaśmalaṃ prāviśad ghoraṃ nirmaryādam avartatad upākrośaṃs tadānyonyaṃ śarair gāḍhaṃ pravejitāḥd antarikṣe gatir yeṣāṃ darśanaṃ cāpy arudhyatad upānighnaṃta subhṛśaṃ goṣu govṛṣabhā ivad yudhiṣṭhiro pi dharmātmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitas tadād vyūhaṃ kṛtvā virāṭasya anvayudhyata pāṇḍavaḥd ātmānaṃ śyenavat kṛtvā tuṇḍam āsīd yudhiṣṭhiraḥd pakṣau yamau ca bhavataḥ puccham āsīd vṛkodaraḥd sahasraṃ nyahanat tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd bhīmasenaḥ susaṃkruddhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥd dvisāhasraṃ rathān vīraḥ paralokaṃ praveśayatd nakulas triśataṃ jaghne sahadevaś catuḥśatama śatānīkaḥ śataṃ hatvā viśālākṣaś catuḥśatamc praviṣṭau mahatīṃ senāṃ trigartānāṃ mahārathaud tau praviśya mahāsenāṃ balavantau yaśasvinaue ārcchetāṃ bahusaṃrabdhau keśākeśi nakhānakhia lakṣayitvā trigartānāṃ tau praviṣṭau rathavrajamc jagmatuḥ sūryadattaś ca madirāśvaś ca pṛṣṭhataḥd śaṅkho virāṭaputras tu maheṣvāso mahābalaḥd vinighnan samare śatrūn praviveśa mahācamūma virāṭas tatra saṃgrāme hatvā pañcaśatān rathānc hayānāṃ ca śatāny atra hatvā pañca mahārathāna caran sa vividhān mārgān ratheṣu rathayūthapaḥc trigartānāṃ suśarmāṇam ārcchad rukmarathaṃ raṇea tau vyāvaharatāṃ tatra mahātmānau mahābalauc anyonyam abhigarjantau goṣṭhe govṛṣabhāv ivad tato rājā trigartānāṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥd matsyaṃ samīyād yattāśvaṃ dvairathena nararṣabhaḥd trigartānāṃ ca mukhyo sau matsyānāṃ ca mahābalaḥd abhīyatur athānyonyaṃ dvairathena nararṣabhad rājasiṃhau susaṃrabdhau virejatur amarṣaṇaud ayudhyanta raṇe vīrāḥ śūrāḥ parighabāhavaḥd kabandhāḥ samare hantuṃ mahāyodhāḥ pracakramuḥd hanyatāṃ hanyatām eva śirāṃsi patitāny apid kabandhān prerayām āsur huṃkāroccāraṇādibhiḥd virāṭaś ca mahāścaryaṃ dṛṣṭvā kautukam āgatamd harṣaṃ lebhe paraṃ rājā mamāpy evaṃvidhā narāḥd kabandhena śataṃ yodhāḥ pātitā raṇamūrdhanid tataḥ kabandhaḥ patitaḥ puṣpavarṣaiḥ sahaiva tud vimānaṃ preritaṃ devair apsarobhiḥ samāvṛtamd samakṣaṃ sarvayodhānāṃ tatrārūḍho divaṃ yayaud na śekur iti saṃkruddhāḥ śūrāḥ kartuṃ parāṅmukhāna tato rathābhyāṃ rathinau vyatiyāya samantataḥc śarān vyasṛjatāṃ śīghraṃ toyadhārā ghanāv ivaa anyonyaṃ cātisaṃrabdhau viceratur amarṣaṇauc kṛtāstrau niśitair bāṇair asiśaktigadābhṛtaua tato rājā suśarmāṇaṃ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥc pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiś cāsya vivyādha caturo hayānd dvābhyāṃ sūtaṃ tu vivyādha ketuṃ ca tribhir āśugaiḥa tathaiva matsyarājānaṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥc pañcāśatā śitair bāṇair vivyādha paramāstravita tataḥ sainyaṃ samāvṛtya matsyarājasuśarmaṇoḥc nābhyajānaṃs tadānyonyaṃ pradoṣe rajasāvṛte vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tamasābhiplute loke rajasā caiva bhāratac vyatiṣṭhan vai muhūrtaṃ tu vyūḍhānīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥa tato ndhakāraṃ praṇudann udatiṣṭhata candramāḥc kurvāṇo vimalāṃ rātriṃ nandayan kṣatriyān yudhia tataḥ prakāśam āsādya punar yuddham avartatac ghorarūpaṃ tatas te sma nāvekṣanta parasparama tataḥ suśarmā traigartaḥ saha bhrātrā yavīyasāc abhyadravan matsyarājaṃ rathavrātena sarvaśaḥa tato rathābhyāṃ praskandya bhrātarau kṣatriyarṣabhauc gadāpāṇī susaṃrabdhau samabhyadravatāṃ hayāna tathaiva teṣāṃ tu balāni tānikruddhāny athānyonyam abhidravantic gadāsikhaḍgaiś ca paraśvadhaiś caprāsaiś ca tīkṣṇāgrasupītadhāraiḥa balaṃ tu matsyasya balena rājāsarvaṃ trigartādhipatiḥ suśarmāc pramathya jitvā ca prasahya matsyaṃvirāṭam ojasvinam abhyadhāvatd mattāv iva vṛṣāv etau gajāv iva madoddhataud siṃhāv iva gajagrāhau śakravṛtrāv ivotthitaud ubhau tulyabalotsāhāv ubhau tulyaparākramaud ubhau tulyāstravikṣepāv ubhau yuddhaviśāradaua tau nihatya pṛthag dhuryāv ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathīb āstāṃ tulyadhanurgrāhau viṣṇukaṃsāv ivoddhataub suśarmā paravīraghno balavān vīryavān gadīc virathaṃ matsyarājānaṃ jīvagrāham agṛhṇatāma tam unmathya suśarmā tu rudatīṃ vadhukām ivac syandanaṃ svaṃ samāropya prayayau śīghravāhanaḥa tasmin gṛhīte virathe virāṭe balavattareb balaṃ sarvaṃ vibhagnaṃ tan nirutsāhaṃ nirāśakamc prādravanta bhayān matsyās trigartair arditā bhṛśamd vidikṣu dikṣu sarvāsu palāyanti ca yānti caa teṣu saṃtrāsyamāneṣu kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc abhyabhāṣan mahābāhuṃ bhīmasenam ariṃdamama matsyarājaḥ parāmṛṣṭas trigartena suśarmaṇāc taṃ mokṣaya mahābāho na gacched dviṣatāṃ vaśama uṣitāḥ smaḥ sukhaṃ sarve sarvakāmaiḥ supūjitāḥb bhīmasena mahābāho gṛhītaṃ taṃ suśarmaṇāb trāyasva mokṣaya kṣipram asmatprītikaraṃ nṛpamc bhīmasena tvayā kāryā tasya vāsasya niṣkṛtiḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd taṃ tathāvādinaṃ tatra bhīmaseno mahābalaḥd abhyabhāṣata durdharṣo raṇamadhye yudhiṣṭhiram bhīmasena uvācaa aham enaṃ paritrāsye śāsanāt tava pārthivac paśya me sumahat karma yudhyataḥ saha śatrubhiḥa svabāhubalam āśritya tiṣṭha tvaṃ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahac ekāntam āśrito rājan paśya me dya parākramama suskandho yaṃ mahāvṛkṣo gadārūpa iva sthitaḥc enam eva samārujya drāvayiṣyāmi śātravān vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa taṃ mattam iva mātaṅgaṃ vīkṣamāṇaṃ vanaspatimc abravīd bhrātaraṃ vīraṃ dharmarājo yudhiṣṭhiraḥa mā bhīma sāhasaṃ kārṣīs tiṣṭhatv eṣa vanaspatiḥc mā tvā vṛkṣeṇa karmāṇi kurvāṇam atimānuṣame janāḥ samavabudhyeran bhīmo yam iti bhārataf mā grahīs tvam imaṃ vṛkṣaṃ siṃhanādaṃ ca mā nadaf imaṃ vṛkṣaṃ gṛhītvā tvaṃ nemāṃ senām abhidravaf vṛkṣaṃ cet tvaṃ nayer vīra vijñāsyati jano dhruvama anyad evāyudhaṃ kiṃ cit pratipadyasva mānuṣamc cāpaṃ vā yadi vā śaktiṃ nistriṃśaṃ vā paraśvadhama yad eva mānuṣaṃ bhīma bhaved anyair alakṣitamc tad evāyudham ādāya mokṣayāśu mahīpatima yamau ca cakrarakṣau te bhavitārau mahābalauc vyūhataḥ samare tāta matsyarājaṃ parīpsataḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd bhrātur vacanam ājñāya bhīmo vṛkṣaṃ visṛjya cad cāpam ādāya saṃprāpto ratham āruhya pāṇḍavaḥd ity uktvā bhīmasenaṃ taṃ svayam eva yudhiṣṭhiraḥd anvayāj javanair aśvaiḥ parīpsan mātsyasattamamd vaiśaṃpāyana uvācad evam uktas tu vegena bhīmaseno mahābalaḥd gṛhītvā tu dhanuḥśreṣṭhaṃ javena sumahājavaḥd vimuñcac charavarṣāṇi satoya iva toyadaḥd taṃ bhīmo bhīmakarmāṇaṃ suśarmāṇam athādravatd virāṭaṃ samavīkṣyainaṃ tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cāvadatd suśarmā cintayām āsa kālāntakayamopamamd tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhāṣantaṃ pṛṣṭhato rathapuṃgavaḥd paśyatāṃ sumahat karma mahad yuddham upasthitamd parāvṛtto dhanur gṛhya suśarmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahad nimeṣāntaramātreṇa bhīmasenena te rathāḥd pātitā bhīmasenena virāṭasya samīpataḥd rathānāṃ ca gajānāṃ ca vājināṃ ca sasādināmd sahasraśatasaṃghātāḥ śūrāṇām ugradhanvināmd pattayo nihatās teṣāṃ gadāṃ gṛhya mahātmanād tad dṛṣṭvā tādṛśaṃ yuddhaṃ suśarmā yuddhadurmadaḥd cintayām āsa manasā kiṃśeṣaṃ hi balasya med aparo dṛśyate sainye purā magno mahābaled ākarṇapūrṇena tadā dhanuṣā pratyadṛśyatad suśarmā sāyakāṃs tīkṣṇān kṣipate ca punaḥ punaḥa tataḥ samastās te sarve turagān abhyacodayanc divyam astraṃ vikurvāṇās trigartān pratyamarṣaṇāḥa tān nivṛttarathān dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavān sā mahācamūḥc vairāṭī paramakruddhā yuyudhe paramādbhutamd trigartāḥ samatikramya vyayudhyanta jayaiṣiṇaḥd tān bhīmasenaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa sahasraṃ nyavadhīt tatra kuntīputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc bhīmaḥ saptaśatān yodhān paralokam adarśayate nakulaś cāpi saptaiva śatāni prāhiṇoc charaiḥa śatāni trīṇi śūrāṇāṃ sahadevaḥ pratāpavānc yudhiṣṭhirasamādiṣṭo nijaghne puruṣarṣabhaḥd tato bhyapatad atyugraḥ suśarmāṇam udāyudhame bhittvā tāṃ mahatīṃ senāṃ trigartānāṃ nararṣabhaf kṣobhayan sarvasainyāni siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgān ivaa tato yudhiṣṭhiro rājā tvaramāṇo mahārathaḥc abhidrutya suśarmāṇaṃ śarair abhyatudad bhṛśama suśarmāpi susaṃkruddhas tvaramāṇo yudhiṣṭhiramc avidhyan navabhir bāṇaiś caturbhiś caturo hayāna tato rājann āśukārī kuntīputro vṛkodaraḥc samāsādya suśarmāṇam aśvān asya vyapothayata pṛṣṭhagopau ca tasyātha hatvā paramasāyakaiḥc athāsya sārathiṃ kruddho rathopasthād apāharata cakrarakṣaś ca śūraś ca śoṇāśvo nāma viśrutaḥc sa bhayād dvairathaṃ dṛṣṭvā traigartaṃ prājahat tadāa tato virāṭaḥ praskandya rathād atha suśarmaṇaḥc gadām asya parāmṛśya tam evājaghnivān balīe sa cacāra gadāpāṇir vṛddho pi taruṇo yathāf tayoḥ sa dṛṣṭvā tatkarma matsyapāṇḍavayor mṛdhef tvaramāṇo rathaṃ tyaktvā padātiḥ prādravad raṇātf palāyamānaṃ traigartaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmo bhyabhāṣataf anena vīryeṇa kathaṃ gās tvaṃ prārthayase balātf rājaputra nivartasva na te yuktaṃ palāyanamf kathaṃ cānucarāṃs tyaktvā śatrumadhye viṣīdasif ity uktaḥ sa tu pārthena suśarmā rathayūthapaḥf tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti bhīmaṃ sa sahasābhyadravad balīf pañcabhis tvarito bhīmaṃ jaghāna samare balīf tāṃ  bāṇān triṇīkṛtya jīvitepsus tato raṇātf prādravat tūrṇam avyagro jīvitepsuḥ suśarmaṇaḥa bhīmas tu bhīmasaṃkāśo rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalīc trigartarājam ādatta siṃhaḥ kṣudramṛgaṃ yathād taṃ bhīmaseno dhāvantam abhyadhāvata vīryavānd utplutyāgatya vegena tadrathe vinipatya cad suśarmaṇaḥ śiro gṛhṇāt punar āśvāsya yudhyataḥd abhidrutya suśarmāṇaṃ keśapakṣe parāmṛśatd samudyamya ca roṣāt taṃ niṣpipeṣa mahītaled padā mūrdhni mahābāhuḥ prāharad vilapiṣyataḥd tasya jānuṃ dadau bhīmo jaghne cainam aratninād sa moham agamad rājā prahāravarapīḍitaḥd taṃ niṣedhayatāṃ bhīmaṃ yamau traigartam āraṇed tadā bhīmo bhisaṃkruddhas tasya darpaṃ nanāśa had ūrdhvam utplutya mārjāra ākhor yadvac chiro ruṣāa tasmin gṛhīte virathe trigartānāṃ mahārathec abhajyata balaṃ sarvaṃ traigartaṃ tadbhayāturama nivartya gās tataḥ sarvāḥ pāṇḍuputrā mahābalāḥc avajitya suśarmāṇaṃ dhanaṃ cādāya sarvaśaḥa svabāhubalasaṃpannā hrīniṣedhā yatavratāḥb mocayitvā virāṭaṃ taṃ pāṇḍavās te hatadviṣaḥb virāṭasya mahātmānaḥ parikleśavināśanāḥb sthitāḥ samakṣaṃ te sarve tv atha bhīmo bhyabhāṣatab nāyaṃ pāpasamācāro matto jīvitum arhatib kiṃ nu śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ yad rājā satataṃ ghṛṇīb gale gṛhītvā rājānam ānīya vivaśaṃ vaśamb tata enaṃ viceṣṭantaṃ baddhvā pārtho vṛkodaraḥb ratham āropayām āsa visaṃjñaṃ pāṃsuguṇṭhitamb abhyetya raṇamadhyastham abhyagacchad yudhiṣṭhiramb darśayām āsa bhīmas tu tām avasthāṃ suśarmaṇaḥb provāca puruṣavyāghro bhīmam āhavaśobhinamb taṃ rājā prāhasad dṛṣṭvā mucyatāṃ vai narādhamaḥb evam ukto bravīd bhīmaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ mahābalamb jīvituṃ cecchase mūḍha hetuṃ te vadataḥ śṛṇub dāso smīti tvayā vācyaṃ saṃsatsu ca sabhāsu cab evaṃ te jīvitaṃ dadyām eṣa yuddhajito vidhiḥb tam uvāca tato jyeṣṭho bhrātā sapraṇayaṃ vacaḥb muñcemam adhamācāraṃ pramāṇaṃ yadi te vayamb dāsabhāvaṃ gato hy eṣa virāṭasya mahīpateḥb adāso gaccha mukto si maivaṃ kārṣīḥ punaḥ kva citb evam ukte tu savrīḍaḥ suśarmāsīd adhomukhaḥb sa mukto bhyetya rājānam abhivādya pratasthivānb pramucya ca suśarmāṇaṃ pāṇḍavās te hatadviṣaḥb svabāhubalasaṃpannā hrīniṣevā yatavratāḥc saṃgrāmaśiraso madhye tāṃ rātriṃ sukhino vasand sa bhīmasenaḥ samare nihatyad śatrūn virāṭasya mahānubhāvaḥd nanāda hṛṣṭo balavān amarṣīd siṃho yathā kṣudramṛgaṃ nihatyaa tato virāṭaḥ kaunteyān atimānuṣavikramānc arcayām āsa vittena mānena ca mahārathānd vacasā caiva sāntvena snehena ca mudānvitaḥ virāṭa uvācaa yathaiva mama ratnāni yuṣmākaṃ tāni vai tathāc kāryaṃ kuruta taiḥ sarve yathākāmaṃ yathāsukhama dadāny alaṃkṛtāḥ kanyā vasūni vividhāni cac manasaś cāpy abhipretaṃ yad vaḥ śatrunibarhaṇāḥa yuṣmākaṃ vikramād adya mukto haṃ svastimān ihac tasmād bhavanto matsyānām īśvarāḥ sarva eva hi vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tathābhivādinaṃ matsyaṃ kauraveyāḥ pṛthak pṛthakc ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve yudhiṣṭhirapurogamāḥa pratinandāma te vākyaṃ sarvaṃ caiva viśāṃ patec etenaiva pratītāḥ smo yat tvaṃ mukto dya śatrubhiḥd yat tvaṃ mukto si śatrubhya etat kāryaṃ hitaṃ hi naḥd na kiṃ cit kāryam asmākaṃ na dhanaṃ mṛgayāmahea athābravīt prītamanā matsyarājo yudhiṣṭhiramb nirbharaḥ prītipūrveṇa harṣagadgadayā girāc punar eva mahābāhur virāṭo rājasattamaḥe ehi tvām abhiṣekṣyāmi matsyarājo stu no bhavāna manasaś cāpy abhipretaṃ yat te śatrunibarhaṇac tat te haṃ saṃpradāsyāmi sarvam arhati no bhavāna ratnāni gāḥ suvarṇaṃ ca maṇimuktam athāpi vāc vaiyāghrapadya viprendra sarvathaiva namo stu tea tvatkṛte hy adya paśyāmi rājyam ātmānam eva cab evam uktas tu matsyena tam abhāṣata pāṇḍavaḥc yataś ca jātaḥ saṃrambhaḥ sa ca śatrur vaśaṃ gataḥd vinayeneti rājānaṃ vadantaṃ tatra saṃsadid dharmarājo mahārāja jagāda sadṛśīṃ girama tato yudhiṣṭhiro matsyaṃ punar evābhyabhāṣatac pratinandāmi te vākyaṃ manojñaṃ matsya bhāṣasea ānṛśaṃsyaparo nityaṃ susukhaḥ satataṃ bhavab punar eva virāṭaś ca rājā kaṅkam abhāṣatab aho śūdrasya karmāṇi valalasya dvijottamab so haṃ śūdreṇa saṃgrāme valalenābhirakṣitaḥb tvatkṛte sarvam evaitad upapannaṃ mamānaghab varaṃ vṛṇīṣva bhadraṃ te brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi teb dadāni te mahāprītyā ratnāny uccāvacāny apib śayanāsanayānāni kanyāś ca samalaṃkṛtāḥb hastyaśvarathasaṃghāś ca rāṣṭrāṇi vividhāni cab vaiśaṃpāyanaḥb tathaiva ca mama prītyā pratigṛhṇa mamāntikeb taṃ tathā vādinaṃ tatra kauravyaḥ pratyabhāṣatab eṣaiva tu mama prītir yat tvaṃ mukto si śatrubhiḥb pratītaś cet punas tuṣṭaḥ pravekṣyasi tadānaghab dāraiḥ putraiś ca saṃśliṣya sā hi prītir mamātulāb suśarmāṇaṃ tu rājendra sabhṛtyabalavāhanamb visarjaya naraśreṣṭha varam etad ahaṃ vṛṇeb evam uktas tu kaṅkena virāṭo rājasattamaḥb pratyuvāca tataḥ kaṅkaṃ suśarmā yātu ceṣṭataḥc gacchantu dūtās tvaritaṃ nagaraṃ tava pārthivae suhṛdāṃ priyam ākhyātuṃ ghoṣayantu ca te jayama tatas tadvacanān matsyo dūtān rājā samādiśatc ācakṣadhvaṃ puraṃ gatvā saṃgrāme vijayaṃ mamaa kumārāḥ samalaṃkṛtya paryāgacchantu me purātc vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi gaṇikāś ca svalaṃkṛtāḥd etad ājñāṃ tataḥ śrutvā rājñā matsyena noditāḥd tām ājñāṃ śirasā kṛtvā prasthitā hṛṣṭamānasāḥd pratyāyāntu ca te sarve nāgarāḥ sarva eva hia te gatvā kevalāṃ rātrim atha sūryodayaṃ pratib evam uktās tathā dūtā rātrau yātvā tu kevalamb tato ntare vai uṣitā dūtāḥ śīghrānuyāyinaḥb nagaraṃ prāviśaṃs te vai sūrye samyag athoditec virāṭasya purābhyāśe dūtā jayam aghoṣayand patākocchrayamālāḍhyaṃ puram apratimaṃ yathā vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa yāte trigartaṃ matsye tu paśūṃs tān svān parīpsatic duryodhanaḥ sahāmātyo virāṭam upayād athaa bhīṣmo droṇaś ca karṇaś ca kṛpaś ca paramāstravitc drauṇiś ca saubalaś caiva tathā duḥśāsanaḥ prabhuḥa viviṃśatir vikarṇaś ca citrasenaś ca vīryavānc durmukho duḥsahaś caiva ye caivānye mahārathāḥa ete matsyān upāgamya virāṭasya mahīpateḥc ghoṣān vidrāvya tarasā godhanaṃ jahrur ojasāa ṣaṣṭiṃ gavāṃ sahasrāṇi kuravaḥ kālayanti tec mahatā rathavaṃśena parivārya samantataḥa gopālānāṃ tu ghoṣeṣu hanyatāṃ tair mahārathaiḥc ārāvaḥ sumahān āsīt saṃprahāre bhayaṃkarea gavādhyakṣas tu saṃtrasto ratham āsthāya satvaraḥc jagāma nagarāyaiva parikrośaṃs tadārtavata sa praviśya puraṃ rājño nṛpaveśmābhyayāt tataḥc avatīrya rathāt tūrṇam ākhyātuṃ praviveśa haa dṛṣṭvā bhūmiṃjayaṃ nāma putraṃ matsyasya māninamc tasmai tat sarvam ācaṣṭa rāṣṭrasya paśukarṣaṇama ṣaṣṭiṃ gavāṃ sahasrāṇi kuravaḥ kālayanti tec tad vijetuṃ samuttiṣṭha godhanaṃ rāṣṭravardhanama rājaputra hitaprepsuḥ kṣipraṃ niryāhi vai svayamc tvāṃ hi matsyo mahīpālaḥ śūnyapālam ihākarota tvayā pariṣado madhye ślāghate sa narādhipaḥc putro mamānurūpaś ca śūraś ceti kulodvahaḥa iṣvastre nipuṇo yodhaḥ sadā vīraś ca me sutaḥb samarthaḥ samare yoddhuṃ kauravaiḥ saha tādṛśaiḥc tasya tat satyam evāstu manuṣyendrasya bhāṣitamd jayaś ca niyato yuddhe kauravāś ca dhruvaṃ hatāḥa āvartaya kurūñ jitvā paśūn paśumatāṃ varac nirdahaiṣām anīkāni bhīmena śaratejasāa dhanuścyutai rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥc dviṣatāṃ bhindhy anīkāni gajānām iva yūthapaḥa pāśopadhānāṃ jyātantrīṃ cāpadaṇḍāṃ mahāsvanāmc śaravarṇāṃ dhanurvīṇāṃ śatrumadhye pravādayad niryāhi nagarāc chīghraṃ rājaputra kim āsyatea śvetā rajatasaṃkāśā rathe yujyantu te hayāḥc dhvajaṃ ca siṃhaṃ sauvarṇam ucchrayantu tavābhibhoḥa rukmapuṅkhāḥ prasannāgrā muktā hastavatā tvayāc chādayantu śarāḥ sūryaṃ rājñām āyur nirodhinaḥa raṇe jitvā kurūn sarvān vajrapāṇir ivāsurānc yaśo mahad avāpya tvaṃ praviśedaṃ puraṃ punaḥa tvaṃ hi rāṣṭrasya paramā gatir matsyapateḥ sutaḥb yathā hi pāṇḍuputrāṇām arjuno jayatāṃ varaḥb evam eva gatir nūnaṃ bhavān viṣayavāsināmc gatimanto bhavantv adya sarve viṣayavāsinaḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd mahājanasamakṣaṃ tu strīmadhye tu viśeṣataḥd gavādhyakṣeṇa saṃproktaṃ vākyaṃ tejaḥpravardhanama strīmadhya uktas tenāsau tad vākyam abhayaṃkaramc antaḥpure ślāghamāna idaṃ vacanam abravīt uttara uvācaa adyāham anugaccheyaṃ dṛḍhadhanvā gavāṃ padamc yadi me sārathiḥ kaś cid bhaved aśveṣu kovidaḥa tam eva nādhigacchāmi yo me yantā bhaven naraḥc paśyadhvaṃ sārathiṃ kṣipraṃ mama yuktaṃ prayāsyataḥa aṣṭāviṃśatirātraṃ vā māsaṃ vā nūnam antataḥc yat tad āsīn mahad yuddhaṃ tatra me sārathir hataḥa sa labheyaṃ yadi tv anyaṃ hayayānavidaṃ naramc tvarāvān adya yātvāhaṃ samucchritamahādhvajama vigāhya tatparānīkaṃ gajavājirathākulamc śastrapratāpanirvīryān kurūñ jitvānaye paśūna duryodhanaṃ śāṃtanavaṃ karṇaṃ vaikartanaṃ kṛpamc droṇaṃ ca saha putreṇa maheṣvāsān samāgatāna vitrāsayitvā saṃgrāme dānavān iva vajrabhṛtc anenaiva muhūrtena punaḥ pratyānaye paśūna śūnyam āsādya kuravaḥ prayānty ādāya godhanamc kiṃ nu śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃ yad ahaṃ tatra nābhavama paśyeyur adya me vīryaṃ kuravas te samāgatāḥc kiṃ nu pārtho rjunaḥ sākṣād ayam asmān prabādhate vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasya tad vacanaṃ strīṣu bhāṣataḥ sma punaḥ punaḥc nāmarṣayata pāñcālī bībhatsoḥ parikīrtanama athainam upasaṃgamya strīmadhyāt sā tapasvinīc vrīḍamāneva śanakair idaṃ vacanam abravītd śrutvā tad arjuno vākyam uttareṇa prabhāṣitamd pāñcālīm arjuno vākyam upāṃśu tad anusmarand atītasamaye kāle priyāṃ bhāryām abhāṣatad drupadasya sutāṃ rājñaḥ pāñcālīṃ rūpasaṃmatāmd satyārjavaguṇopetāṃ bhartuḥ priyahitaiṣiṇīmd uttarāṃ brūhi pāñcāli gatvā kṣipraṃ śucismited ayaṃ kila purā yuddhe khāṇḍave savyasācinaḥd sārathiḥ pāṇḍuputrasya pārthasya tu bṛhannalād vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd mahāñ jayo bhaved yuddhe sā ced yantā bṛhannalād sā coditā tadā tena arjunena śucismitād pāñcālī ca tadāgamya uttarāyā niveśanamd jñātvā tu samayān muktaṃ candraṃ rāhumukhād ivad yudhiṣṭhiraṃ dharmaparaṃ satyārjavapathe sthitamd amarṣayantī tad duḥkhaṃ kṛṣṇā kamalalocanād uttarām āha vacanaṃ sakhimadhye vilāsinīa yo sau bṛhadvāraṇābho yuvā supriyadarśanaḥb draupadīb yo yaṃ yuvā vāraṇayūthapopamob bṛhannalāsmīti jane bhyabhāṣatab purā hi pārthasya sa sārathis tadāb dhanurdharāṇāṃ pravarasya manyec bṛhannaḍeti vikhyātaḥ pārthasyāsīt sa sārathiḥd etena vai sārathinā tadārjunaḥd sa devagandharvamahoragāsurānd sarvāṇi bhūtāny ajayat sa vīryavānd atarpayac cāpi hiraṇyaretasamd yad asya saṃsthām api tasya saṃyuged jānāmi vīryaṃ paravīryamadhyagaḥd saṃgṛhya raśmīn api vārya vīryavānd ādāya cāpaṃ prayayau rathe sthitaḥd na sarvabhūtāni na devadānavāḥd na cāpi sarve kuravaḥ samāgatāḥd dhanaṃ hareyus tava jātu dhanvinod bṛhannalā tūttarasārathir yadia dhanuṣy anavaraś cāsīt tasya śiṣyo mahātmanaḥc dṛṣṭapūrvo mayā vīra carantyā pāṇḍavān pratia yadā tat pāvako dāvam adahat khāṇḍavaṃ mahatc arjunasya tadānena saṃgṛhītā hayottamāḥa tena sārathinā pārthaḥ sarvabhūtāni sarvaśaḥc ajayat khāṇḍavaprasthe na hi yantāsti tādṛśaḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd tataḥ sairandhrisahitā uttarā bhrātur abravītd abhyarthayemāṃ sārathye vīra śīghraṃ bṛhannalāmd śikṣitaiṣāṃ hi sārathye nartane gītavādited sairandhry āha mahāprājña stuvantī vai bṛhannalāmd śrutvottarottarāvākyaṃ sairandhryā samudīritamd saṃdhārya manasā samyak sairandhrīṃ punar abravītd uttaraḥd sairandhri jānāsi mama vrataṃ hid klībo na eṣa puruṣaḥ svayaṃ hid nāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi bṛhannalāṃ śubhed vaktuṃ svayaṃ yaccha hayān mametid sairandhrīd bhayakāle tu saṃprāpte na vrataṃ nāvrataṃ punaḥd yathā duḥkhaṃ pratarati kartuṃ yuktaṃ cared budhaḥd iti dharmavidaḥ prāhus tasmād vācyā bṛhannalāa yeyaṃ kumārī suśroṇī bhaginī te yavīyasīc asyāḥ sa vacanaṃ vīra kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥa yadi vai sārathiḥ sa syāt kurūn sarvān asaṃśayamc jitvā gāś ca samādāya dhruvam āgamanaṃ bhaveta evam uktaḥ sa sairandhryā bhaginīṃ pratyabhāṣatac gaccha tvam anavadyāṅgi tām ānaya bṛhannaḍāma sā bhrātrā preṣitā śīghram agacchan nartanāgṛhamc yatrāste sa mahābāhuś channaḥ satreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca sā prādravat kāñcanamālyadhāriṇī jyeṣṭhena bhrātrā prahitā yaśasvinī sudakṣiṇā vedivilagnamadhyā sā padmapatrābhanibhā śikhaṇḍinī tanvī śubhāṅgī maṇicitramekhalā matsyasya rājño duhitā śriyā vṛtā tan nartanāgāram arālapakṣmā śatahradā megham ivānvapadyata sā hastihastopamasaṃhatorūḥ svaninditā cārudatī sumadhyamā āsādya taṃ vai varamālyadhāriṇī pārthaṃ śubhā nāgavadhūr iva dvipam sā ratnabhūtā manasaḥ priyārcitā sutā virāṭasya yathendralakṣmīḥ sudarśanīyā pramukhe yaśasvinī prītyābravīd arjunam āyatekṣaṇā susaṃhatoruṃ kanakojjvalatvacaṃ pārthaḥ kumārīṃ sa tadābhyabhāṣata kim āgamaḥ kāñcanamālyadhāriṇi mṛgākṣi kiṃ tvaṃ tvariteva bhāmini kiṃ te mukhaṃ sundari na prasannam ācakṣva tattvaṃ mama śīghram aṅgane bhrātur niyogaṃ tu niśamya subhrūḥ śubhānanā hāṭakaratnabhūṣaṇā savajramuktāmaṇihemakuṇḍalā mṛdukramā bhrātṛniyogacoditā pradakṣiṇāvartatanuḥ śikhaṇḍinī padmānanā padmadalāyatākṣī vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa tāṃ dṛṣṭvā viśālākṣīṃ rājaputrīṃ sakhīṃ sakhāc prahasann abravīd rājan kutrāgamanam ity utaa tam abravīd rājaputrī samupetya nararṣabhamc praṇayaṃ bhāvayantī sma sakhīmadhya idaṃ vacaḥd uvāca tvarayā yuktā cottarā madhurākṣarama gāvo rāṣṭrasya kurubhiḥ kālyante no bṛhannaḍec tān vijetuṃ mama bhrātā prayāsyati dhanurdharaḥa naciraṃ ca hatas tasya saṃgrāme rathasārathiḥc tena nāsti samaḥ sūto yo sya sārathyam ācareta tasmai prayatamānāya sārathyarthaṃ bṛhannaḍec ācacakṣe hayajñāne sairandhrī kauśalaṃ tavad arjunasya kilāsīs tvaṃ sārathir dayitaḥ purād tvayājayat sahāyena pṛthivīṃ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥa sā sārathyaṃ mama bhrātuḥ kuru sādhu bṛhannaḍec purā dūrataraṃ gāvo hriyante kurubhir hi naḥa athaitad vacanaṃ me dya niyuktā na kariṣyasic praṇayād ucyamānā tvaṃ parityakṣyāmi jīvitama evam uktas tu suśroṇyā tayā sakhyā paraṃtapaḥc jagāma rājaputrasya sakāśam amitaujasaḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd sā vajravaiḍūryavikārakuṇḍalād vinidrapadmotpalapatragandhinīd prasannatārādhipasaṃnibhānanād pārthaṃ kumārī vacanaṃ babhāṣed haranti vittaṃ kuravaḥ pitur med śataṃ sahasrāṇi gavāṃ bṛhannaled sā bhrātur aśvān mama saṃyamasvad purā pare dūrataraṃ haranti gāḥd sairandhrir ākhyāti bṛhannale tvāṃd suśikṣitāṃ saṃgrahaṇe rathāśvayoḥd ahaṃ mariṣyāmi na me tra saṃśayod mayā vṛtā tatra na ced gamiṣyasid tathā niyukto naradevakanyayād narottamaḥ prītamanā dhanaṃjayaḥd uvāca pārthaḥ śubhamandayā girād śubhānanāṃ śukladatīṃ śucismitāmd gacchāmi yatrecchasi cāruhāsinid hutāśanaṃ prajvalitaṃ vrajāmi vād icchāmi te haṃ varagātri jīvitaṃd karomi kiṃ te priyam adya sundarid na matkṛte drakṣyasi tat puraṃ priyed vaivasvataṃ pretapater mahābhayamd sa evam uktvā kuruvīrapuṃgavod vilāsinīṃ śukladatīṃ śucismitāmd bṛhannalārūpavibhūṣitānanod virāṭaputrasya samīpam āvrajatd tam āvrajantaṃ varabhūṣaṇair vṛtaṃd mahāprabhaṃ vāraṇayūthapopamamd gajendrabāhuṃ kamalāyatekṣaṇaṃd kavāṭavakṣaḥsthalam unnatāṃsamd tam āgataṃ pārtham amitrakarśanaṃd mahābalaṃ nāgam iva pramāthinamd vairāṭir āmantrya tato bṛhannalāṃd gavāṃ ninīṣan padam uttaro bravīta taṃ sā vrajantaṃ tvaritaṃ prabhinnam iva kuñjaramc anvagacchad viśālākṣī śiśur gajavadhūr ivaa dūrād eva tu taṃ prekṣya rājaputro bhyabhāṣatac tvayā sārathinā pārthaḥ khāṇḍave gnim atarpayata pṛthivīm ajayat kṛtsnāṃ kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥc sairandhrī tvāṃ samācaṣṭa sā hi jānāti pāṇḍavāna saṃyaccha māmakān aśvāṃs tathaiva tvaṃ bṛhannaḍec kurubhir yotsyamānasya godhanāni parīpsataḥa arjunasya kilāsīs tvaṃ sārathir dayitaḥ purāc tvayājayat sahāyena pṛthivīṃ pāṇḍavarṣabhaḥd devendrasārathir vīro mātaliḥ khyātavikramaḥd suhotro jāmadagnyasya viṣṇor yantā ca dārukaḥd aruṇaḥ sūryayantā ca sumantro daśarathasya cad sarve sārathayaḥ khyātā na bṛhannalayā samāḥd ity ukto haṃ ca sairandhryā tena tvām āhvayāmi vaid āhūtā tvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ yoddhuṃ yāhi bṛhannaled dūrād dūrataraṃ gāvo bhavanti kurubhir hṛtāḥa evam uktā pratyuvāca rājaputraṃ bṛhannaḍāc kā śaktir mama sārathyaṃ kartuṃ saṃgrāmamūrdhania gītaṃ vā yadi vā nṛttaṃ vāditraṃ vā pṛthagvidhamc tat kariṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sārathyaṃ tu kuto mayi uttara uvācaa bṛhannaḍe gāyano vā nartano vā punar bhavac kṣipraṃ me ratham āsthāya nigṛhṇīṣva hayottamānd tvaṃ nartako vā yadi vāpi gāyakaḥd kṣipraṃ tanutraṃ paridhatsva bhānumatd abhīkṣṇam āhus tava karma pauruṣaṃd striyaḥ praśaṃsanti mamādya cāntiked vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd ity evam uktvā nṛpasūnusattamasd tadā smayitvārjunam abhyanandayatd athottaraḥ pāraśavaṃ śatākṣimatd suvarṇacitraṃ parigṛhya bhānumatd bṛhannalāyai pradadau svayaṃ tadād virāṭaputraḥ paravīraghātined tadājñayā mātsyasutasya vīryavānd akartukāmeva samādade tadād bṛhannalād yady asti ca raṇe śauryaṃ śaktiḥ syād dviṣatāṃ vadhed ahaṃ tvām abhigacchāmi yatra tvaṃ yāsi tatra bhoḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa tatra narmasaṃyuktam akarot pāṇḍavo bahuc uttarāyāḥ pramukhataḥ sarvaṃ jānann ariṃdamaa ūrdhvam utkṣipya kavacaṃ śarīre pratyamuñcatac kumāryas tatra taṃ dṛṣṭvā prāhasan pṛthulocanāḥd tam ādadānaṃ pramadā jahāsired hy adhomukhaṃ vīravaro bhyahārayatd tatas tiraścīnakṛtaṃ sapatnahād hy adhomukhaṃ kavacam athābhyakarṣayatd samyak prajānann api satyavikramod hy ajñātavat sarvakurupravīraḥd ūrdhvaṃ kṣipan vīravaro bhyahārayatd punaś ca yatnāt kavacaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥd evaṃprakārāṇi bahūni kurvatid tasmin kumāryaḥ pramadā jahāsirea sa tu dṛṣṭvā vimuhyantaṃ svayam evottaras tataḥc kavacena mahārheṇa samanahyad bṛhannaḍāmd tathā vikurvantam amitrakarśanaṃd naivottaraḥ paryabhavad dhanaṃjayamd taṃ rājaputraḥ samanāhayat svayaṃd jāmbūnadāntena śubhena varmaṇād kṛśānutaptapratimena bhāsvatād jājvalyamānena sahasraraśmināa sa bibhrat kavacaṃ cāgryaṃ svayam apy aṃśumatprabhamc dhvajaṃ ca siṃham ucchritya sārathye samakalpayatd athāsya śīghraṃ prasamīkṣya yojayadd rathe hayān kāñcanajālasaṃvṛtānd suvarṇajālāntarayoktṛbhūṣaṇānd siṃhaṃ ca sauvarṇam upāśrayad rathea dhanūṃṣi ca mahārhāṇi bāṇāṃś ca rucirān bahūnb āyudhāni ca vai tatra rathopasthe ca saṃnyasatc ādāya prayayau vīraḥ sa bṛhannaḍasārathiḥa athottarā ca kanyāś ca sakhyas tām abruvaṃs tadāc bṛhannaḍe ānayethā vāsāṃsi rucirāṇi naḥa pāñcālikārthaṃ sūkṣmāṇi citrāṇi vividhāni cac vijitya saṃgrāmagatān bhīṣmadroṇamukhān kurūna atha tā bruvatīḥ kanyāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇḍunandanaḥc pratyuvāca hasan pārtho meghadundubhiniḥsvanaḥa yady uttaro yaṃ saṃgrāme vijeṣyati mahārathānc athāhariṣye vāsāṃsi divyāni rucirāṇi caa evam uktvā tu bībhatsus tataḥ prācodayad dhayānc kurūn abhimukhāñ śūro nānādhvajapatākinaḥd athottaro varma mahāprabhāvaṃd suvarṇavaiḍūryapariṣkṛtaṃ dṛḍhamd āmucya vīraḥ prayayau rathottamaṃd dhanaṃjayaṃ sārathinaṃ pragṛhyad tam uttaraṃ vīkṣya rathottame sthitaṃd bṛhannaḍāyāḥ sahitaṃ mahābhujamd striyaś ca kanyāś ca dvijāś ca suvratāḥd pradakṣiṇaṃ cakrur athocuraṅganāḥd yad arjunasyarṣabhatulyagāminaḥd purābhavat khāṇḍavadāhamaṅgalamd kurūn samāsādya raṇe bṛhannaḍed sahottareṇāstu tad adya maṅgalam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa sa rājadhānyā niryāya vairāṭiḥ pṛthivīṃjayaḥc prayāhīty abravīt sūtaṃ yatra te kuravo gatāḥa samavetān kurūn yāvaj jigīṣūn avajitya vaic gāś caiṣāṃ kṣipram ādāya punar āyāmi svaṃ purama tatas tāṃś codayām āsa sadaśvān pāṇḍunandanaḥc te hayā narasiṃhena coditā vātaraṃhasaḥe ālikhanta ivākāśam ūhuḥ kāñcanamālinaḥa nātidūram atho yātvā matsyaputradhanaṃjayauc avekṣetām amitraghnau kurūṇāṃ balināṃ balame śmaśānam abhito gatvā āsasāda kurūn athaf tāṃ śamīm anvavīkṣetāṃ vyūḍhānīkāṃś ca sarvaśaḥa tad anīkaṃ mahat teṣāṃ vibabhau sāgarasvanamc sarpamāṇam ivākāśe vanaṃ bahulapādapama dadṛśe pārthivo reṇur janitas tena sarpatāc dṛṣṭipraṇāśo bhūtānāṃ divaspṛṅ narasattamaa tad anīkaṃ mahad dṛṣṭvā gajāśvarathasaṃkulamc karṇaduryodhanakṛpair guptaṃ śāṃtanavena caa droṇena ca saputreṇa maheṣvāsena dhīmatāb teṣāṃ tat sainyam atulaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayavivardhanamc hṛṣṭaromā bhayodvignaḥ pārthaṃ vairāṭir abravīta notsahe kurubhir yoddhuṃ romaharṣaṃ hi paśya mec bahupravīram atyugraṃ devair api durāsadame pratiyoddhuṃ na śakṣyāmi kurusainyam anantakama nāśaṃse bhāratīṃ senāṃ praveṣṭuṃ bhīmakārmukāmb devair api sahendreṇa na śakyaṃ kiṃ punar naraiḥc rathanāgāśvakalilāṃ pattidhvajasamākulāme dṛṣṭvaiva hi parān ājāv ātmā pravyathatīva mea yatra droṇaś ca bhīṣmaś ca kṛpaḥ karṇo viviṃśatiḥc aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca somadatto tha bāhlikaḥa duryodhanas tathā vīro rājā ca rathināṃ varaḥc dyutimanto maheṣvāsāḥ sarve yuddhaviśāradāḥd mattā iva mahānāgā yuktadhvajapatākinaḥd nītimanto maheṣvāsāḥ sarvāstrakṛtaniścayāḥd durjayāḥ sarvasainyānāṃ devair api savāsavaiḥd patākinaś ca mātaṅgāḥ sadhvajāś ca mahārathāḥd viprakīrṇāḥ kṛtodyogā vājinaś citrabhūṣitāḥd tāñ jetuṃ samare śūrān durbuddhir aham āgataḥa dṛṣṭvaiva hi kurūn etān vyūḍhānīkān prahāriṇaḥc hṛṣitāni ca romāṇi kaśmalaṃ cāgataṃ mama vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa aviyāto viyātasya maurkhyād dhūrtasya paśyataḥb dṛṣṭvā tu mahatīṃ senāṃ kurūṇāṃ dṛḍhadhanvināmc paridevayate mandaḥ sakāśe savyasācinaḥa trigartān me pitā yātaḥ śūnye saṃpraṇidhāya māmc sarvāṃ senām upādāya na me santīha sainikāḥa so ham eko bahūn bālaḥ kṛtāstrān akṛtaśramaḥc pratiyoddhuṃ na śakṣyāmi nivartasva bṛhannaḍed vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd taṃ tathāvādinaṃ tatra bībhatsuḥ pratyabhāṣatad saṃprahasya punas taṃ vai sarvalokamahārathaḥ arjuna uvācaa bhayena dīnarūpo si dviṣatāṃ harṣavardhanaḥc na ca tāvat kṛtaṃ kiṃ cit paraiḥ karma raṇājirea svayam eva ca mām āttha vaha māṃ kauravān pratic so haṃ tvāṃ tatra neṣyāmi yatraite bahulā dhvajāḥa madhyam āmiṣagṛdhrāṇāṃ kurūṇām ātatāyināmc neṣyāmi tvāṃ mahābāho pṛthivyām api yudhyatāmd samudram iva gambhīraṃ kurusainyam ariṃdamad strīsakāśe pratijñāya puruṣāṇāṃ hi śṛṇvatāmd vikatthamāno niryātvā brūhi kiṃ nātra budhyasea tathā strīṣu pratiśrutya pauruṣaṃ puruṣeṣu cac katthamāno bhiniryāya kimarthaṃ na yuyutsasea na ced vijitya gās tās tvaṃ gṛhān vai pratiyāsyasic prahasiṣyanti vīra tvāṃ narā nāryaś ca saṃgatāḥa aham apy atra sairandhryā stutaḥ sārathyakarmaṇic na hi śakṣyāmy anirjitya gāḥ prayātuṃ puraṃ pratia stotreṇa caiva sairandhryās tava vākyena tena cac kathaṃ na yudhyeyam ahaṃ kurūn sarvān sthiro bhava uttara uvācaa kāmaṃ harantu matsyānāṃ bhūyāṃsaṃ kuravo dhanamb agnido garadaś caiva śastrapāṇir dhanāpahaḥb kṣetradāraharaś caiva ṣaḍete hy ātatāyinaḥb ātatāyinam āyāntam api vedāṅgapāragamb jighāṃsantaṃ jighāṃsīyān na naro brahmahā bhavetb saṃgrāmeṇa na me kāryaṃ gāvo gacchantu cāpi meb śūnyaṃ me nagaraṃ cāpi pituś caiva bibhemy ahamb kṣīraṃ vā dadhi vājyaṃ vā takraṃ vā na pibāmy ahamb āranālaṃ hi pāsyāmi na me gobhiḥ prayojanamb nagaraṃ ca pravekṣyāmi paśyatas te bṛhannaleb nivartaya rathaṃ tūrṇaṃ hṛdayaṃ me vidīryateb varaṃ kālena jīvakṣabhun na me gobhiḥ prayojanamb yady ahaṃ jīvamānas tu gacchāmi nagaraṃ prati c prahasantu ca māṃ nāryo narā vāpi bṛhannaḍed bhojanaṃ gorasair hīnaṃ kāñjikenāpy ataḥ paramd bhokṣye haṃ bahubhir vāpi yāsye bālo mṛter bhayāt vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa ity uktvā prādravad bhīto rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalīc tyaktvā mānaṃ sa mandātmā visṛjya saśaraṃ dhanuḥ bṛhannaḍovācaa naiṣa pūrvaiḥ smṛto dharmaḥ kṣatriyasya palāyanamc śreyas te maraṇaṃ yuddhe na bhītasya palāyanam vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktvā tu kaunteyaḥ so vaplutya rathottamātc tam anvadhāvad dhāvantaṃ rājaputraṃ dhanaṃjayaḥe dīrghāṃ veṇīṃ vidhunvānaḥ sādhu rakte ca vāsasīf vikramantaṃ padanyāsair namayann iva bhūtalama vidhūya veṇīṃ dhāvantam ajānanto rjunaṃ tadāc sainikāḥ prāhasan ke cit tathārūpam avekṣya tama taṃ śīghram abhidhāvantaṃ saṃprekṣya kuravo bruvanb sainikāḥb ko yaṃ dhāvaty asaṃgena pūrvaṃ muktvā rathottamamc ka eṣa veṣapracchanno bhasmaneva hutāśanaḥa kiṃ cid asya yathā puṃsaḥ kiṃ cid asya yathā striyaḥb ity evaṃ sainikāḥ prāhur droṇas tān idam abravītb ācāryaḥ kurupāṇḍūnāṃ matau śukrāṅgiropamaḥb kiṃ vicāreṇa vaḥ kāryam etenānusṛtena vaib dhāvantam anudhāvaṃś ca nirbhayo bhayaviplutamb veṇīkalāpaṃ nirdhūya pravibhāti nararṣabhaḥc sārūpyam arjunasyeva klībarūpaṃ bibharti cad rūpeṇa pārthasadṛśaḥ strīveṣasamalaṃkṛtaḥa tad evaitac chirogrīvaṃ tau bāhū parighopamauc tadvad evāsya vikrāntaṃ nāyam anyo dhanaṃjayāta amareṣv iva devendro mānuṣeṣu dhanaṃjayaḥc ekaḥ ko smān upāyāyād anyo loke dhanaṃjayātd droṇena caivam ukte tu karṇaḥ provāca buddhimāna ekaḥ putro virāṭasya śūnye saṃnihitaḥ purec sa eṣa kila niryāto bālabhāvān na pauruṣātd klībaṃ vai sārathiṃ kṛtvā niryāto nagarād bahiḥa satreṇa nūnaṃ channaṃ hi carantaṃ pārtham arjunamb te hi naḥ pratisaṃyātuṃ saṃgrāme na hi śaknuyuḥb katham ekataras teṣāṃ samastān yodhayet kurūnc uttaraḥ sārathiṃ kṛtvā niryāto nagarād bahiḥa sa no manye dhvajān dṛṣṭvā bhīta eṣa palāyatic taṃ nūnam eṣa dhāvantaṃ jighṛkṣati dhanaṃjayaḥd eko smān anuyāty eṣa nānyo loke dhanaṃjayātd sārathiṃ hy uttaraṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ yoddhum ihecchatia iti sma kuravaḥ sarve vimṛśantaḥ pṛthak pṛthakc na ca vyavasituṃ kiṃ cid uttaraṃ śaknuvanti ted duryodhana uvācedaṃ sainikān rathasattamānd arjuno vāsudevo vā rāmaḥ pradyumna eva vād te hi naḥ pratisaṃyoddhuṃ saṃgrāme na hi śaknuyuḥd katham ekataras teṣāṃ samastān yodhayet kurūnd anyo vai klībaveṣeṇa yady āgacched gavāṃ padamd śarais tīkṣṇair arpayitvā pātayiṣyāmi bhūtalee channaṃ tathā taṃ satreṇa pāṇḍavaṃ prekṣya bhārataf arjunaṃ neti cety enaṃ na vyavasyanti te punaḥf iti sma kuravaḥ sarve mantrayanti mahārathāḥf dṛḍhavedhī mahāsattvaḥ śakratulyaparākramaḥf abhyāgacchati ced yoddhuṃ sarvaṃ saṃśayitaṃ balamf na cāpy anyataraṃ tatra vyavasyanti dhanaṃjayāta uttaraṃ tu pradhāvantam anudrutya dhanaṃjayaḥc gatvā padaśataṃ tūrṇaṃ keśapakṣe parāmṛśatd mā mā gṛhāṇa bhadraṃ te dāso haṃ te bṛhannaled iti vādinam evāśu dhāvantaṃ tarasāgrahītd virāṭaputraṃ bībhatsur balavān arimardanaḥa so rjunena parāmṛṣṭaḥ paryadevayad ārtavatb mā mā māraya bhadraṃ te muñca mām emi me gṛhamb muñca māṃ muñca muñceti tatpādāv agrahīd bruvanb darśayitvā tataḥ sarvān adaśat so ṅguliṃ nṛpab mā bhais tvam iti pārthena prārthitaḥ paryadevayatc bahulaṃ kṛpaṇaṃ caiva virāṭasya sutas tadād uttara uvācad śṛṇuyās tvaṃ hi kalyāṇi bṛhannaḍe sumadhyamed nivartaya rathaṃ śīghraṃ jīvan bhadrāṇi paśyatid grāmāś caturdaśa tathā pūrṇāś ca dhanagokulaiḥd dadāmy etad dhanaṃ tubhyaṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍed aśvānāṃ tu sahasre dve śubhrāṇāṃ hemamālināmd sarvalakṣaṇayuktānāṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍed uttaraḥd suvarṇamaṇimuktānāṃ yad yad icchasi dadmi ted hastino śvān rathān gāvaḥ striyaś ca samalaṃkṛtāḥa śātakumbhasya śuddhasya śataṃ niṣkān dadāmi tea   śreṣṭhasya rajatasya caa dadāmi śataniṣkaṃ te muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannalec maṇīn aṣṭau ca vaiḍūryān hemabaddhān mahāprabhāna hemadaṇḍapraticchannaṃ rathaṃ yuktaṃ ca suvrajaiḥc mattāṃś ca daśa mātaṅgān muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍed ṣaṣṭiṃ svalaṃkṛtāḥ kanyā grāmam ekaṃ dadāmi ted muñca māṃ tvaṃ bhṛśaṃ dīnaṃ vihvalaṃ bhayakampitamd gamiṣyāmi puraṃ ṣaṇḍha draṣṭuṃ mātaram arditāmd mātsyasya putro bālo haṃ tena cāsmi sukhoṣitaḥd mātṛpārśvaśayāno ham aspṛṣṭātapavāyumānd adṛṣṭabalayuddho haṃ kutas te kuravaḥ kutaḥd mātṛpārśvaṃ gamiṣyāmi muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaled pralayārṇavasaṃkāśaṃ dṛśyate kauravaṃ balamd strīṇāṃ madhye ham ajñānād vīryaśauryāṅkitāṃ giramd uktavān madagarveṇa ko jetuṃ śaknuyāt kurūnd amuktvā vā yadi nayer mariṣyāmi tavāgrataḥd pragṛhyaitad dhanaṃ sarvaṃ muñca māṃ tvaṃ bṛhannaḍed āranālena jīviṣye na me gobhiḥ prayojanamd arjuna uvācad jīvan prāpsyāmi gā hy anyā nivartasva bṛhannaḍed yaśo hi kalpāntaśataikasākṣid na jīvitaṃ kuñjarakarṇalolamd kṣitipālasūno bhava raṅgamadhyed uttara uvācad lajjāmahe saṃgararaṅgabhaṅgātd yā kīrtir utsarpati dehanāśed dhig duḥkhadāṃ mūlavināśinīṃ tāmd vikrīya dehaṃ draviṇena ko nud yātrākṛtaṃ devakule karoti vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evamādīni vākyāni vilapantam acetasamc prahasya puruṣavyāghro rathasyāntikam ānayata athainam abravīt pārtho bhayārtaṃ naṣṭacetasamb arjunaḥb ahaṃ yotsyāmi kauravyair hayān saṃyaccha cottarab ādadānaḥ kimarthaṃ tvaṃ palāyanaparobhavaḥb yudhyasva kauravaiḥ sārdhaṃ vijayas te bhaviṣyatib yasya yantāsmy ahaṃ yuddhe saṃyacchāmi hayottamānb rājño vā rājaputrasya tasya nityaṃ jayo dhruvaḥb sarvathottara yudhyasva yantrā sākaṃ mayā kurūnb jitvā mahīṃ yaśaḥ prāpya bhokṣyase sakalām imāmb hato pi prāpsyase svargaṃ na śreyas te palāyanamb adya sarvān kurūñ jitvā yathā jayam avāpsyasib tathāhaṃ prayatiṣye tra sahāyo tra mato hy ahamb saṃyacchāmi hayān yasya na sa bhītaḥ palāyatic yadi notsahase yoddhuṃ śatrubhiḥ śatrukarśanae ehi me tvaṃ hayān yaccha yudhyamānasya śatrubhiḥa prayāhy etad rathānīkaṃ madbāhubalarakṣitaḥc apradhṛṣyatamaṃ ghoraṃ guptaṃ vīrair mahārathaiḥa mā bhais tvaṃ rājaputrāgrya kṣatriyo si paraṃtapab kathaṃ puruṣaśārdūla śatrumadhye viṣīdasic ahaṃ vai kurubhir yotsyāmy avajeṣyāmi te paśūna praviśyaitad rathānīkam apradhṛṣyaṃ durāsadamc yantā bhūs tvaṃ naraśreṣṭha yotsye haṃ kurubhiḥ sahad śūrān samaracaṇḍāṃś ca nayiṣye yamasādanama evaṃ bruvāṇo bībhatsur vairāṭim aparājitaḥc samāśvāsya muhūrtaṃ tam uttaraṃ bharatarṣabhaa tata enaṃ viceṣṭantam akāmaṃ bhayapīḍitamc ratham āropayām āsa pārthaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥd kurūn abhimukhaṃ pārthaḥ prayayau śīghravāhanaḥd yathendro dānavān hantuṃ prayāti ca samātaliḥd tam āropya rathopasthe vilapantaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥd gāṇḍīvaṃ dhanur ādātum upāyāt tāṃ śamīṃ pratid uttaraṃ sa samāśvāsya kṛtvā yantāram arjunaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa taṃ dṛṣṭvā klībaveṣeṇa rathasthaṃ narapuṃgavamc śamīm abhimukhaṃ yāntaṃ ratham āropya cottarama bhīṣmadroṇamukhās tatra kurūṇāṃ rathasattamāḥc vitrastamanasaḥ sarve dhanaṃjayakṛtād bhayāta tān avekṣya hatotsāhān utpātān api cādbhutānc guruḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho bhāradvājo bhyabhāṣataa calāś ca vātāḥ saṃvānti rūkṣāḥ paruṣaniḥsvanāḥc bhasmavarṇaprakāśena tamasā saṃvṛtaṃ nabhaḥa rūkṣavarṇāś ca jaladā dṛśyante dbhutadarśanāḥc niḥsaranti ca kośebhyaḥ śastrāṇi vividhāni caa śivāś ca vinadanty etā dīptāyāṃ diśi dāruṇāḥc hayāś cāśrūṇi muñcanti dhvajāḥ kampanty akampitāḥa yādṛśāny atra rūpāṇi saṃdṛśyante bahūny apic yattā bhavantas tiṣṭhantu syād yuddhaṃ samupasthitama rakṣadhvam api cātmānaṃ vyūhadhvaṃ vāhinīm apic vaiśasaṃ ca pratīkṣadhvaṃ rakṣadhvaṃ cāpi godhanamd etāvad uktvā vacanaṃ bhīṣmam ālokya cābravītd nadīja laṅkeśavanāriketurd nagāhvayo nāma nagārisūnuḥd gatyā sureśaḥ kva cid aṅganevad gurur babhāṣe vacanaṃ tad evad ity uktvā saṃjñayā droṇas tūṣṇīm āsīd viśāṃ pated bhāradvājavacaḥ śrutvā gāṅgeyaḥ saṃjñayābravītd atītaṃ cakram asmākaṃ viṣayāntaram āgatāḥd atītaḥ samayaś cokto hy asmābhir yaḥ sabhātaled na bhayaṃ śatrutaḥ kāryaṃ śaṅkāṃ tyaja nararṣabhad duryodhanam athālokya saṃjñayā droṇa abravītd devavratenaivam ukte vacane hitakāriṇāa eṣa vīro maheṣvāsaḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥb gavām arthe hi vikrāntaḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥb nadīja laṅkeśavanāriketurb nagāhvayo nāma nagārisūnuḥb eṣo ṅganāveṣadharaḥ kirīṭīb jitvāva yaṃ neṣyati cādya gā vaḥc āgataḥ klībaveṣeṇa pārtho nāsty atra saṃśayaḥa sa eṣa pārtho vikrāntaḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥc nāyuddhena nivarteta sarvair api marudgaṇaiḥd ye jetāro mahīpānām amunā bahavo hatāḥd yasmiṃs tejo mahat kṛtsnaṃ nirbharocchvasitaṃ bhavetd yena me dakṣiṇā dattā baddhvā drupadam ojasād viddhvā viyadgataṃ lakṣyaṃ vinirjitya ca pārthivānd nirjitānena pāñcālī purānena svayaṃvared khāṇḍave yena saṃtṛpto vahnir jitvā surāsurānd pariṇītā subhadrā ca yena nirjitya yādavānd nirjito yena yuddhena tripurāriḥ smarārdanaḥd gatvā triviṣṭapaṃ yena jitendrā dānavā yudhid nivātakavacā rājan dānavānāṃ trikoṭayaḥd nirjitāḥ kālakeyāś ca hiraṇyapuravāsinaḥd yena tvaṃ mocito baddhaś citrasenena tadvaned yena gatvottaraṃ meror ānināya mahad dhanamd yājito dharmasūnuś ca nṛpān sarvān vijitya cad yasmiñ śauryaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca tejo dhairyaṃ parākramaḥd audāryaṃ caiva gāmbhīryaṃ hrīḥ śrīr dharmo dayārjavamd evamādiguṇopetaḥ so yaṃ pārtho na saṃśayaḥa kleśitaś ca vane śūro vāsavena ca śikṣitaḥc amarṣavaśam āpanno yotsyate nātra saṃśayaḥa nehāsya pratiyoddhāram ahaṃ paśyāmi kauravāḥc mahādevo pi pārthena śrūyate yudhi toṣitaḥd kirātaveṣapracchanno girau himavati prabhuḥd ity evaṃ vādinaṃ droṇaṃ karṇaḥ kruddho bravīd vacaḥ karṇa uvācaa sadā bhavān phalgunasya guṇair asmān vikatthasec na cārjunaḥ kalā pūrṇā mama duryodhanasya vā duryodhana uvācaa yady eṣa pārtho rādheya kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ bhaven mamac jñātāḥ punaś cariṣyanti dvādaśānyān hi vatsarāna athaiṣa kaś cid evānyaḥ klībaveṣeṇa mānavaḥc śarair enaṃ suniśitaiḥ pātayiṣyāmi bhūtale vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tasmin bruvati tad vākyaṃ dhārtarāṣṭre paraṃtapec bhīṣmo droṇaḥ kṛpo drauṇiḥ pauruṣaṃ tad apūjayan vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tāṃ śamīm upasaṃgamya pārtho vairāṭim abravītc sukumāraṃ samājñātaṃ saṃgrāme nātikovidamd ehi bhūmiṃjayāruhya vairāṭe mahatīṃ śamīma samādiṣṭo mayā kṣipraṃ dhanūṃṣy avaharottarac nemāni hi tvadīyāni soḍhuṃ śakṣyanti me balama bhāraṃ vāpi guruṃ hartuṃ kuñjaraṃ vā pramarditumc mama vā bāhuvikṣepaṃ śatrūn iha vijeṣyataḥd naibhiḥ kāmam ahaṃ kartuṃ karma vaijayikaṃ tv ihad atisūkṣmāṇi hrasvāni sarvāṇi ca mṛdūni cad āyudhāni mahābāho tavaitāni paraṃtapaa tasmād bhūmiṃjayāroha śamīm etāṃ palāśinīmc asyāṃ hi pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ dhanūṃṣi nihitāny utaa yudhiṣṭhirasya bhīmasya bībhatsor yamayos tathāc dhvajāḥ śarāś ca śūrāṇāṃ divyāni kavacāni caa atra caitan mahāvīryaṃ dhanuḥ pārthasya gāṇḍivamc ekaṃ śatasahasreṇa saṃmitaṃ rāṣṭravardhanama vyāyāmasaham atyarthaṃ tṛṇarājasamaṃ mahatc sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ śatrusaṃbādhakārakama suvarṇavikṛtaṃ divyaṃ ślakṣṇam āyatam avraṇamc alaṃ bhāraṃ guruṃ voḍhuṃ dāruṇaṃ cārudarśaname tādṛśāny eva sarvāṇi balavanti dṛḍhāni caf pradhānāni viśiṣṭāni durdarśāni bhavanty utaf arjunenaivam uktas tu vairāṭiḥ pratyabhāṣata uttara uvācaa asmin vṛkṣe kilodbaddhaṃ śarīram iti naḥ śrutamc tad ahaṃ rājaputraḥ san spṛśeyaṃ pāṇinā kathama naivaṃvidhaṃ mayā yuktam ālabdhuṃ kṣatrayonināc mahatā rājaputreṇa mantrayajñavidā satād spṛśāmīha śarīraṃ ced apy asyāṃ śokavarjitaḥa spṛṣṭavantaṃ śarīraṃ māṃ śavavāham ivāśucimc kathaṃ vā vyavahāryaṃ vai kurvīthās tvaṃ bṛhannaḍed vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd tam uvāca tataḥ śūraḥ pārthaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥd dāyādaṃ sarvamatsyānāṃ kule jātaṃ viśāradamd jānāmi tvāṃ mahāprājña śubhaṃ jātyā kulena cad kathaṃ nu pāpakaṃ karma brūyāṃ tvāhaṃ paraṃtapa bṛhannaḍovācaa vyavahāryaś ca rājendra śuciś caiva bhaviṣyasic dhanūṃṣy etāni mā bhais tvaṃ śarīraṃ nātra vidyatea dāyādaṃ matsyarājasya kule jātaṃ manasvinamc kathaṃ tvā ninditaṃ karma kārayeyaṃ nṛpātmaja vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa evam uktaḥ sa pārthena rathāt praskandya kuṇḍalīc āruroha śamīvṛkṣaṃ vairāṭir avaśas tadāa tam anvaśāsac chatrughno rathe tiṣṭhan dhanaṃjayaḥb avāropaya vṛkṣāgrād dhanūṃṣy etāni mā bibhaḥc pariveṣṭanam eteṣāṃ kṣipraṃ caiva vyapānudad so pahṛtya mahārhāṇi dhanūṃṣi pṛthuvakṣasāmd pariveṣṭanapatrāṇi vimucya samupānayata tathā saṃnahanāny eṣāṃ parimucya samantataḥc apaśyad gāṇḍivaṃ tatra caturbhir aparaiḥ sahaa teṣāṃ vimucyamānānāṃ dhanuṣām arkavarcasāmc viniśceruḥ prabhā divyā grahāṇām udayeṣv ivaa sa teṣāṃ rūpam ālokya bhoginām iva jṛmbhatāmc hṛṣṭaromā bhayodvignaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyatac   pravepitatanus tadāc arjunena samāśvastaḥc   kiṃ cid dhṛṣṭo nṛpātmajaḥc teṣāṃ saṃdarśanābhyāsaṃ sparśābhyāsaṃ punaḥ punaḥc āmīlya punar unmīlya spṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā cakāra saḥc samyag dṛṣṭvā tadāśvastaḥd tad upaśrutya śatrughnaḥ sa tadārjunam abravītd sārathe kim idaṃ śete nāgendro vāpi vā dhanuḥa saṃspṛśya tāni cāpāni bhānumanti bṛhanti cac vairāṭir arjunaṃ rājann idaṃ vacanam abravīt uttara uvāca na dṛṣṭaṃ na śrutaṃ citraṃ dhanuṣo rūpam īdṛśama bindavo jātarūpasya śataṃ yasmin nipātitāḥc sahasrakoṭi sauvarṇāḥ kasyaitad dhanur uttamama vāraṇā yasya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe bhāsanti daṃśitāḥc supārśvaṃ sugrahaṃ caiva kasyaitad dhanuruttamama tapanīyasya śuddhasya ṣaṣṭir yasyendragopakāḥc pṛṣṭhe vibhaktāḥ śobhante kasyaitad dhanur uttamama sūryā yatra ca sauvarṇās trayo bhāsanti daṃśitāḥc tejasā prajvalanto hi kasyaitad dhanur uttamama śālabhā yatra sauvarṇās tapanīyavicitritāḥc suvarṇamaṇicitraṃ ca kasyaitad dhanur uttamama ime ca kasya nārācāḥ sahasrā lomavāhinaḥc samantāt kaladhautāgrā upāsaṅge hiraṇmayea vipāṭhāḥ pṛthavaḥ kasya gārdhrapatrāḥ śilāśitāḥc hāridravarṇāḥ sunasāḥ pītāḥ sarvāyasāḥ śarāḥa kasyāyam asitāvāpaḥ pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥc varāhakarṇavyāmiśraḥ śarān dhārayate daśaa kasyeme pṛthavo dīrghāḥ sarvapāraśavāḥ śarāḥc śatāni sapta tiṣṭhanti nārācā rudhirāśanāḥa kasyeme śukapatrābhaiḥ pūrvair ardhaiḥ suvāsasaḥc uttarair āyasaiḥ pītair hemapuṅkhaiḥ śilāśitaiḥd gurubhārasaho divyaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥd hemapuṅkho gārdhapatraḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥa kasyāyaṃ sāyako dīrghaḥ śilīpṛṣṭhaḥ śilīmukhaḥc vaiyāghrakośe nihito hemacitratsarur mahāna suphalaś citrakośaś ca kiṅkiṇīsāyako mahānc kasya hematsarur divyaḥ khaḍgaḥ paramanirvraṇaḥa kasyāyaṃ vimalaḥ khaḍgo gavye kośe samarpitaḥc hematsarur anādhṛṣyo naiṣadhyo bhārasādhanaḥa kasya pāñcanakhe kośe sāyako hemavigrahaḥc pramāṇarūpasaṃpannaḥ pīta ākāśasaṃnibhaḥa kasya hemamaye kośe sutapte pāvakaprabhec nistriṃśo yaṃ guruḥ pītaḥ saikyaḥ paramanirvraṇaḥd kasyāyam asitaḥ khaḍgo hemabindubhir āvṛtaḥd āśīviṣasamasparśaḥ parakāyaprabhedanaḥd gurubhārasaho divyaḥ sapatnānāṃ bhayapradaḥd uttaraḥd sārathe kim idaṃ divyaṃ nāgo vā yadi vā dhanuḥd sauvarṇāny atra padmāni śatapatrāṇi bhāgaśaḥd kuśāgnipratitaptāni bhānumanti bṛhanti cad a bindavaś cātra sauvarṇā maṇiprotāḥ samantataḥd śaśisūryaprabhāḥ pṛṣṭhe bhānti rukmapariṣkṛtāḥd pughpāṇy atra suvarṇāni śatapatrāṇi bhāgaśaḥd vismāpanīyarūpaṃ ca bhīmaṃ bhīmapradarśanamd nīlotpalanibhaṃ kasya śātakumbhapariṣkṛtamd ab ṛṣabhā yasya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti śṛṅgiṇaḥd tālapramāṇaṃ kasyedaṃ maṇirukmavibhūṣitamd hāṭakasya suvarṇasya yasmiñ śākhāmṛgā daśad durānamaṃ mahad dīrghaṃ surūpaṃ duṣpradharṣaṇamd kasyedam īdṛśaṃ citraṃ dhanuḥ sarve ca daṃsitāḥd candrārkavimalā bhāsaḥ surūpāḥ supradarśanāḥd haṃsāḥ pṛṣṭhe śritā yasya kuśāgnipratimārciṣaḥd śārṅgagāṇḍīvasadṛśaṃ kasyedaṃ sārathe dhanuḥd caturthaṃ kāñcanavapur bhāti vidyudgaṇopamamd nīlotpalitam acchidraṃ jātarūpaprabhaṃ dhanuḥd matsyā yasya hiraṇyasya pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti saṃcitāḥd śakracāpopamaṃ divyaṃ kasyedaṃ sārathe dhanuḥd ucchritaṃ phaṇivad dīrghaṃ sāravattvād durānamamd c sahasragodhāḥ sauvarṇā dvīpinaś ca caturdaśad barhiṇaś cātra sauvarṇāḥ śatacandrārkabhūṣaṇāḥd jāmbūnadavicitrāṅgaṃ kasyedaṃ pañcamaṃ dhanuḥd ab kasyeme kṣuranārācāḥ sahasraṃ lomavāpinaḥd pakṣiṇas tīkṣṇatuṇḍāgrāḥ kasyeme niśitāḥ śarāḥd ab vipāṭāḥ pṛthavaḥ kasya gṛdhrapatrārdhavājitāḥd cab varāhakarṇās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ kasyeme rucirāḥ śarāḥd vajrāśanisamasparśā vaiśvānarasamārciṣaḥd suvarṇapuṅkhās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ kasya saptaśataṃ śarāḥd a kasyāyaṃ sāyako dīrgho gavye kośe ca daṃsitaḥd kasya daṇḍo dṛḍhaḥ ślakṣṇo ruciro yaṃ prakāśated c vaiyāghrakośaḥ kasyāyaṃ divyaḥ khaḍgo mahāprabhaḥd ab kasyāyam asir āvāpe pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥd ab kasyāyaṃ nirmalaḥ khaḍgo dvīpicarmādhivāsitaḥd nīlotpalasavarṇo yaṃ kasya khaḍgaḥ pṛthur mahānd mṛgendracarmāvasitas tīkṣṇadhāraḥ sunirmalaḥd ṛṣabhājinakośas tu kasya khaḍgo mahān ayamd yasyāpidhāne dṛśyante sūryāḥ pañca pariṣkṛtāḥd a kasyāyaṃ vipulaḥ khaḍgaḥ śṛṅgatsarumanoharaḥd nihitaḥ pārṣate kośe tailadhautaḥ samāhitaḥd c pramāṇavarṇayuktaś ca kasya khaḍgo mahān ayamd naitena pratividdhaḥ sañ jīvet kaś cana kuñjaraḥd viprakṣiptās tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrā upāsaṅge hiraṇmayed hāridravarṇāḥ kasyeme śitāḥ pañcaśataṃ śarāḥd āśīviṣasamasparśā gatau cājihmagā dṛḍhāḥd yasyāpidhāne dṛśyante śārdūlāḥ kāñcanāḥ śubhāḥa nirdiśasva yathātattvaṃ mayā pṛṣṭā bṛhannaḍec vismayo me paro jāto dṛṣṭvā sarvam idaṃ mahat bṛhannaḍovāca vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ uttareṇaivam uktas tu pārtho vairāṭim abravīt mṛdvyā pratyāyayan vācā bhītaṃ śaṅkāvaśaṃ gatama yan māṃ pūrvam ihāpṛcchaḥ śatrusenānibarhaṇamc gāṇḍīvam etat pārthasya lokeṣu viditaṃ dhanuḥd abhedyam ajaraṃ śrīmad divyam acchedyam avraṇama sarvāyudhamahāmātraṃ śātakumbhapariṣkṛtamc etat tad arjunasyāsīd gāṇḍīvaṃ paramāyudhama yat tac chatasahasreṇa saṃmitaṃ rāṣṭravardhanamc yena devān manuṣyāṃś ca pārtho viṣahate mṛdhed citram uccāvacair varṇaiḥ ślakṣṇam āyatam avraṇama devadānavagandharvaiḥ pūjitaṃ śāśvatīḥ samāḥc etad varṣasahasraṃ tu brahmā pūrvam adhārayata tato nantaram evātha prajāpatir adhārayatc trīṇi pañcaśataṃ caiva śakro śīti ca pañca caa somaḥ pañcaśataṃ rājā tathaiva varuṇaḥ śatamb tasmāc ca varuṇād agniḥ premṇā prāhṛtya tac chubhamb agninā pratibhāvyena dattaṃ pārthāya gāṇḍivamc pārthaḥ pañca ca ṣaṣṭiṃ ca varṣāṇi śvetavāhanaḥa mahāvīryaṃ mahad divyam etat tad dhanur uttamamb etan mām anusaṃprāptaṃ varuṇāc cārudarśanamb nīlotpalanibhaṃ rājñaḥ kauravyasya mahātmanaḥb bindavaś cāsya sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe sādhu niyojitāḥc pūjitaṃ suramartyeṣu bibharti paramaṃ vapuḥd tālapramāṇaṃ bhīmasya maṇirukmavibhūṣitamd durānamaṃ mahad dīrghaṃ surūpaṃ duṣpradharṣaṇama supārśvaṃ bhīmasenasya jātarūpagrahaṃ dhanuḥb sahasragodhā hairaṇyā dvīpinaś ca caturdaśab ṛṣabhāś cāpi sauvarṇāḥ pṛṣṭhe tiṣṭhanti śṛṅgiṇaḥc yena pārtho jayat kṛtsnāṃ diśaṃ prācīṃ paraṃtapaḥd pṛṣṭhe vibhaktāḥ śobhante kuśāgnipratibhāvitāḥa indragopakacitraṃ ca yad etac cāruvigrahamc rājño yudhiṣṭhirasyaitad vairāṭe dhanur uttamama sūryā yasmiṃs tu sauvarṇāḥ prabhāsante prabhāsinaḥc tejasā prajvalanto vai nakulasyaitad āyudhama śalabhā yatra sauvarṇās tapanīyavicitritāḥc etan mādrīsutasyāpi sahadevasya kārmukamd tapanīyavicitraṃ ca vairāṭe nākulaṃ dhanuḥa ye tv ime kṣurasaṃkāśāḥ sahasrā lomavāhinaḥc ete rjunasya vairāṭe śarāḥ sarpaviṣopamāḥa ete jvalantaḥ saṃgrāme tejasā śīghragāminaḥc bhavanti vīrasyākṣayyā vyūhataḥ samare ripūnd ghorāgrā dīrgharūpāś ca girīṇām api dāraṇāḥa ye ceme pṛthavo dīrghāś candrabimbārdhadarśanāḥc ete bhīmasya niśitā ripukṣayakarāḥ śarāḥa hāridravarṇā ye tv ete hemapuṅkhāḥ śilāśitāḥc nakulasya kalāpo yaṃ pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥa yenāsau vyajayat kṛtsnāṃ pratīcīṃ diśam āhavec kalāpo hy eṣa tasyāsīn mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥa ye tv ime bhāskarākārāḥ sarvapāraśavāḥ śarāḥc ete citrāḥ kriyopetāḥ sahadevasya dhīmataḥa ye tv ime niśitāḥ pītāḥ pṛthavo dīrghavāsasaḥc hemapuṅkhās triparvāṇo rājña ete mahāśarāḥa yas tv ayaṃ sāyako dīrghaḥ śilīpṛṣṭhaḥ śilīmukhaḥc arjunasyaiṣa saṃgrāme gurubhārasaho dṛḍhaḥa vaiyāghrakośas tu mahān bhīmasenasya sāyakaḥc gurubhārasaho divyaḥ śātravāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaraḥa suphalaś citrakośaś ca hematsarur anuttamaḥc nistriṃśaḥ kauravasyaiṣa dharmarājasya dhīmataḥa yas tu pāñcanakhe kośe nihitaś citrasevanec nakulasyaiṣa nistriṃśo gurubhārasaho dṛḍhaḥa yas tv ayaṃ vimalaḥ khaḍgo gavye kośe samarpitaḥc sahadevasya viddhy enaṃ sarvabhārasahaṃ dṛḍhamd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd evam ākhyātavāṃs tatra svāyudhāni paraṃtapaḥd virāṭaputrāya tadā pārthaḥ satyaparākramaḥd a barhiṇaś cātra sauvarṇāḥ śatacandrārkabhūṣaṇāḥd nakulasya dhanus tv etan mādrīputrasya dhīmataḥd etena sadṛśaṃ citraṃ dhanuś caitad yavīyasaḥd a hāridravarṇaṃ rājñaś ca kauravyasya mahātmanaḥd vipāṭā bhīmasenasya girīṇām api dāraṇāḥd suprabhāḥ sumahākāyās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ sukṛtā dṛḍhāḥd bhīmena prahitā hy ete vāraṇānāṃ nivāraṇāḥd suvarṇavarṇā rucirāḥ kāladaṇḍopamāḥ śubhāḥd c nakulasya śarā hy ete vajrāśanisamaprabhāḥd yāṃś ca tvaṃ pṛcchase dīrghān samadhārān samāhitānd d varāhakarṇās tīkṣṇāgrāḥ sahadevasya te śarāḥd a yas tv ayaṃ sāyako divyo gavye kośe ca daṃsitaḥd d pārthasyāstram idaṃ ghoraṃ sarvabhārasahaṃ mahatd yas tv ayaṃ nirmalaḥ khaḍgo dvīpicarmaṇi daṃsitaḥd rājño yudhiṣṭhirasyāyaṃ kuntīputrasya dhīmataḥd ad vaiyāghrakośo bhīmasya pañcaśārdūlalakṣaṇaḥd vāraṇānāṃ sudṛptānāṃ śikṣitaḥ skandhaśātaned nīlotpalasavarṇābhaḥ khaḍgaḥ pārthasya dhīmataḥd mṛgendracarmapihitas tīkṣṇadhāraḥ samāhitaḥd darśanīyaḥ sutīkṣṇāgraḥ kuntīputrasya dhīmataḥd c arjunasyaiṣa nistriṃśaḥ parasainyāgradūṣaṇaḥd a yas tv ayaṃ pārṣate kośe prakṣipto ruciratsaruḥd c nakulasyaiṣa nistriṃśo vaiśvānarasamaprabhaḥd a yas tv ayaṃ piṅgalaḥ khaḍgaś citro maṇimayatsaruḥd cd sahadevasya khaḍgo yaṃ bhārasāho tidaṃsitaḥd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd bhīmasyāyaṃ mahādaṇḍaḥ sarvāmitravināśanaḥd bhedato hy arjunas tūrṇaṃ kathayām āsa tattvataḥd āyudhāni kalāpāṃś ca nistriṃśāṃś cātulaprabhānd anyat tu sahadevasya dhanuḥ śreṣṭhaṃ mahaujasaḥd kvāsau pracchannavāsānāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahātmanāmd nyastāny atra mahārhāṇi vratasiddhim upeyuṣāmd ity uttaraṃ tu tat sarvam arjunas tattvato bravīt uttara uvācaa suvarṇavikṛtānīmāny āyudhāni mahātmanāmc rucirāṇi prakāśante pārthānām āśukāriṇāmd vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd etasminn antare pārthaṃ mūḍhātmā na vyajānatad virāṭaputraḥ pramukhe papraccha punar eva tua kva nu svid arjunaḥ pārthaḥ kauravyo vā yudhiṣṭhiraḥc nakulaḥ sahadevaś ca bhīmasenaś ca pāṇḍavaḥd kva nu te pāṇḍavāḥ śūrāḥ saṃgrāmeṣv aparājitāḥd eṣām imāni divyāni śriyā dīvyanti bhānti cad kasmin vasanti te deśe dharmajñā bandhuvatsalāḥd kva dharmarājaḥ kauravyo dharmaputro yudhiṣṭhiraḥd bhīmasenārjunau cāpi sarve te mātulā mamad nakulaḥ sahadevo vā sarvāstrakuśalo raṇed dharmaśīlaś ca dharmātmā dharmavān dharmavit sudhīḥd dharmādhyakṣo dharmavrato dharmajño dharmamūrtimānd dharmaniṣṭho dharmakartā dharmagoptā sudharmakṛtd satyārjavakṣamādhāro ghṛṇī dharmaparāyaṇaḥa sarva eva mahātmānaḥ sarvāmitravināśanāḥc rājyam akṣaiḥ parākīrya na śrūyante kadā canaa draupadī kva ca pāñcālī strīratnam iti viśrutāc jitān akṣais tadā kṛṣṇā tān evānvagamad vanamd utsṛjya dharmarājyaṃ te na śrūyante vanaṃ gatāḥd pāṇḍavān yadi jānīṣe kva nu te dharmacāriṇaḥd kva cādya nivasantīti satyaṃ brūhi bṛhannaled vaiśaṃpāyanaḥd tataḥ prahasya bībhatsuḥ kaunteyaḥ śvetavāhanaḥd uvāca rājaputraṃ tam uttaraṃ śṛṇu me vacaḥd kimartham āgatāny atra śastrāstrāṇi mahātmanāmd kathaṃ jñātāni bhavatā tathā me brūhi śobhaned tataḥ prahasya kaunteyo rājaputram uvāca had mā bhais tvaṃ rājaśārdūla sarvaṃ te varṇayāmy ahamd nātra bhetavyam adyāpi rājaputra yathā tathād vayaṃ te pāṇḍavā nāma vanavāsasya pāragāḥd atīte dvādaśe varṣe channavāsam ihoṣitāḥd tasmād aśaṅkitamanāḥ śṛṇuṣva mahitottara arjuna uvācaa aham asmy arjunaḥ pārthaḥ sabhāstāro yudhiṣṭhiraḥc ballavo bhīmasenas tu pitus te rasapācakaḥa aśvabandho tha nakulaḥ sahadevas tu gokulec sairandhrīṃ draupadīṃ viddhi yatkṛte kīcakā hatāḥd bhīmasenena durvṛttaḥ saha bhrātṛbhir āhaved śrutvaitad vacanaṃ jiṣṇor vismayasphāritekṣaṇaḥd paśyann animiṣaḥ pārthaṃ śanair vācam uvāca ha uttara uvācaa daśa pārthasya nāmāni yāni pūrvaṃ śrutāni mec prabrūyās tāni yadi me śraddadhyāṃ sarvam eva te arjuna uvācaa hanta te haṃ samācakṣe daśa nāmāni yāni meb vairāṭe śṛṇu tāni tvaṃ yāni pūrvaṃ śrutāni teb ekāgramānaso bhūtvā śṛṇu sarvaṃ samāhitaḥb īśāno vidadhe devas tridivasyeśvaro divib tāni loke pravṛttāni vairāṭe śṛṇu tattvataḥc arjunaḥ phalguno jiṣṇuḥ kirīṭī śvetavāhanaḥe bībhatsur vijayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥf etāni mama nāmāni sthāpitāni surottamaiḥ uttara uvāca guṇato daśa nāmāni samavetāni pāṇḍave caranti loke khyātāni viditāni mamānaghaa kenāsi vijayo nāma kenāsi śvetavāhanaḥc kirīṭī nāma kenāsi savyasācī kathaṃ bhavāna arjunaḥ phalguno jiṣṇuḥ kṛṣṇo bībhatsur eva cac dhanaṃjayaś ca kenāsi prabrūhi mama tattvataḥe śrutā me tasya vīrasya kevalā nāmahetavaḥf tatsarvaṃ yadi me brūyāḥ śraddadhyāṃ sarvam eva tef itas tataś calaty etan mano me cañcalaṃ tvayif arjuno vā bhavān neti vada śīghraṃ bṛhannale arjuna uvācaa sarvāñ janapadāñ jitvā vittam ācchidya kevalamc madhye dhanasya tiṣṭhāmi tenāhur māṃ dhanaṃjayama abhiprayāmi saṃgrāme yad ahaṃ yuddhadurmadānc nājitvā vinivartāmi tena māṃ vijayaṃ viduḥa śvetāḥ kāñcanasaṃnāhā rathe yujyanti me hayāḥc saṃgrāme yudhyamānasya tenāhaṃ śvetavāhanaḥd kirīṭaṃ sūryasaṃkāśaṃ bhrājate me śirogatamd raṇamadhye rathasthasya sūryapāvakasaṃnibhama uttarābhyāṃ ca pūrvābhyāṃ phalgunībhyām ahaṃ divāc jāto himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe tena māṃ phalgunaṃ viduḥd yo mamāṅge vraṇaṃ kuryān mama jyeṣṭhasya paśyataḥd yudhiṣṭhirasya rudhiraṃ darśayed vā kadā canad parābhavam ahaṃ tasya kule kuryāṃ na saṃśayaḥa purā śakreṇa me dattaṃ yudhyato dānavarṣabhaiḥc kirīṭaṃ mūrdhni sūryābhaṃ tena māhuḥ kirīṭinamd acchedyaṃ ruciraṃ citraṃ jāmbūnadapariṣkṛtamd indradattam anāhāryaṃa na kuryāṃ karma bībhatsaṃ yudhyamānaḥ kathaṃ canac tena devamanuṣyeṣu bībhatsur iti māṃ viduḥa ubhau me dakṣiṇau pāṇī gāṇḍīvasya vikarṣaṇeb dhanuṣāhaṃ samāyuktaḥ śaravarṣaṃ sṛjāmi cab bhujau me bhavataḥ saṃkhye parasainyavināśanec tena devamanuṣyeṣu savyasācīti māṃ viduḥa pṛthivyāṃ caturantāyāṃ varṇo me durlabhaḥ samaḥc karomi karma śuklaṃ ca tena mām arjunaṃ viduḥa ahaṃ durāpo durdharṣo damanaḥ pākaśāsaniḥc tena devamanuṣyeṣu jiṣṇunāmāsmi viśrutaḥd mātā mama pṛthā nāma tena māṃ pārtham abruvand devadānavagandharvān piśācoragarākṣasānd ahaṃ purā raṇe jitvā khāṇḍave gnim atarpayamd hutāśanaṃ tarpayitvā sahitaḥ śārṅgadhanvanād triviṣṭapagatau dṛṣṭvā pitāmahamaheśvaraud mūrcchayā patitaṃ bhūmāv āgatau devasattamaud dṛṣṭvā tau varadau devau saṃjñāṃ labdhvotthitaṃ purād mūrdhnābhipraṇataṃ bhūmau tau tadā varadau varaud kṛṣṇety ekādaśaṃ nāma prītyā me tatra cakratuḥd tuṣṭau ca mama vīryeṇa karmaṇā cābhirādhitaud sarvadevaiḥ parivṛtau bhūyo māṃ svayam ūcatuḥd varaṃ tāta vṛṇīṣveti yat prārthayasi pāṇḍavad tato ham astrāṇy alabhaṃ divyāni ca dṛḍhāni cad brāhmaṃ pāśupataṃ caiva sthūṇākarṇaṃ ca durjayamd aindraṃ vāruṇam āgneyaṃ vāyavyam atha vaiṣṇavamd tato ham ajayaṃ bhūyo rathenaindreṇa durjayānd mātaliṃ sārathiṃ kṛtvā nivātakavacān raṇed avadhyakavacān devair varadattān mahāsurānd tisraḥ koṭīr dānavānāṃ saṃyugeṣv anivartināmd eko nirjitya saṃgrāme bhūyo devān atoṣayamd tato me bhagavān indraḥ kirīṭam adadāt svayamd devāś ca śaṅkham adaduḥ śatrusainyanivāraṇamd ahaṃ pāre samudrasya hiraṇyapuravāsināmd hatvā ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi jayaṃ saṃprāptavān ahamd asaṃbhrānto rathe tiṣṭhan sahasreṣu śateṣu cad śatrumadhye durādharṣo na muhyanti ca me diśaḥd ahaṃ gandharvarājena hriyamāṇaṃ suyodhanamd bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaṃ tāta gandharvaiḥ samare jitamd caturdaśa sahasrāṇi hatvā cainam amocayamd mā bhair vigatasaṃtrāsaḥ kurūn etān samāgatānd suyodhanasya miṣataḥ karṇasya ca kṛpasya cad pitāmahasya bhīṣmasya drauṇer droṇasya ca svayamd sarvān eva kurūñ jitvā pratyāneṣyāmi te paśūna kṛṣṇa ity eva daśamaṃ nāma cakre pitā mamac kṛṣṇāvadātasya sataḥ priyatvād bālakasya vaid sthito smi yattaḥ saṃgrāme vairāṭe vyetu te bhayamd etac chrutvā prahṛṣṭātmā vismayotphullalocanaḥ vaiśaṃpāyana uvācaa tataḥ pārthaṃ sa vairāṭir abhyavādayad antikātb tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā vairāṭiḥ pārṣatottamab prahṛṣṭaromā hṛṣṭo brāhmaṇaṃ kṛpamd lakṣayāmy aham ācāryaṃ bhayād bhaktiṃ gataṃ ripaud bhītena hi na yoddhavyam ahaṃ yotsye dhanaṃjayamd nanu vāruṇam āgneyaṃ yāmyaṃ vāyavyam eva cad astraṃ brahmaśiraś caiva sattvahīnaś ca te vṛthād mitrakāryaṃ kṛtam idaṃ pitāputrair mahārathaiḥd bhartṛpiṇḍaś ca nirdiṣṭo yatheṣṭaṃ gantum arhathad bhikṣāṃ harasva tvaṃ nityaṃ yajñān anucarasva cad āmantraṇaṃ hi bhuṅkṣvādya māsmān gṛhamd tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā aśvatthāmā pratāpavānd uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣṭho duryodhanam avekṣya cad yattāḥ sarve rathaśreṣṭhaṃ parivārya samantataḥd ṣaḍrathāḥ parikīryantāṃ vajrapāṇim ivāsurāḥ kruddho duryodhanam atarjayata prāpya dyūtena ko rājyaṃ kṣatriyas toṣṭum arhatic tathā nṛśaṃsarūpeṇa yathānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥd yad vṛttaṃ prākṛtaiś cīrṇaṃ loke sadbhir vigarhitama tathāvāpteṣu vitteṣu ko vikatthed vicakṣaṇaḥb buddhimān nītimān rājā kṣatriyo yadi vetaraḥc nikṛtyā vañcanāyogaiś caran vaitaṃsiko yathāa katamad dvairathaṃ yuddhaṃ yatrājaiṣīr dhanaṃjayamc nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca dhanaṃ yeṣāṃ tvayā hṛtama yudhiṣṭhiro jitaḥ kasmin bhīmaś ca balināṃ varaḥc indraprasthaṃ tvayā kasmin saṃgrāme nirjitaṃ purāa tathaiva katamaṃ yuddhaṃ yasmin kṛṣṇā jitā tvayāc ekavastrā sabhāṃ nītā duṣṭakarman rajasvalāa mūlam eṣāṃ mahat kṛttaṃ sārārthī candanaṃ yathāc karma kārayithāḥ śūra tatra kiṃ viduro bravīta yathāśakti manuṣyāṇāṃ śamam ālakṣayāmahec anyeṣāṃ caiva sattvānām api kīṭapipīlikea draupadyās taṃ parikleśaṃ na kṣantuṃ pāṇḍavo rhatic duḥkhāya dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ prādurbhūto dhanaṃjayaḥa tvaṃ punaḥ paṇḍito bhūtvā vācaṃ vaktum ihecchasic vairāntakaraṇo jiṣṇur na naḥ śeṣaṃ kariṣyatia naiṣa devān na gandharvān nāsurān na ca rākṣasānc bhayād iha na yudhyeta kuntīputro dhanaṃjayaḥa yaṃ yam eṣo bhisaṃkruddhaḥ saṃgrāme bhipatiṣyatic vṛkṣaṃ garuḍavegena vinihatya tam eṣyatia punaḥ sṛṣṭo maghavatā vajraḥ prapatann iva parvatea etasminn antare tatra mahāvīryaparākramaḥb arjunaṃ prati saṃrabdhaḥ kṛpaḥ paramadurjayaḥc ājagāma mahāsattvaḥ kṛpaḥ śastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥe arjunaṃ tyaktvā kṛpasya ratham uttamamf ājagāmārjunas tūrṇaṃ sūryavaiśvānaraprabhama tau rathau sūryasaṃkāśau yotsyamānau mahābalauc śāradāv iva jīmūtau vyarocetāṃ vyavasthitaud tataḥ śāradvatas tūrṇaṃ pārthaṃ daśabhir āśugaiḥd vivyādha paravīraghnaṃ niśitair marmabhedibhiḥa pārtho pi viśrutaṃ loke gāṇḍīvaṃ paramāyudhamc vikṛṣya cikṣepa bahūn nārācān marmabhedinaḥd kṛpaś ca dhanur ādāya tathaivārjunam abhyayāta tān aprāptāñ śitair bāṇair nārācān raktabhojanānc kṛpaś ciccheda pārthasya śataśo tha sahasraśaḥd jīmūta iva gharmānte śaravarṣaṃ vimuñcatid nandayan suhṛdaḥ sarvān pratyayudhyata phalgunamd vikṛṣya balavac cāpaṃ pāṇḍavo bhīmavikramaḥa tataḥ pārthaś ca saṃkruddhaś citrān mārgān pradarśayanc diśaḥ saṃchādayan bāṇaiḥ pradiśaś ca mahārathaḥa ekacchāyam ivākāśaṃ prakurvan sarvataḥ prabhuḥc pracchādayad ameyātmā pārthaḥ śaraśataiḥ kṛpamd udgataḥ samaye megho dhārābhir iva parvatama sa śarair arpitaḥ kruddhaḥ śitair agniśikhopamaiḥb kṛpo babhūva samare vidhūmo gnir iva jvalanc tūrṇaṃ śarasahasreṇa pārtham apratimaujasame arpayitvā mahātmānaṃ nanāda samare kṛpaḥa tataḥ kanakapuṅkhāgrair vīraḥ saṃnataparvabhiḥb dhanur ādāya vivyādha pārthaṃ daśabhir āśugaiḥb bibheda samare pārthaḥ kṛpasya dhvajam uttamamb tataḥ paścān mahātejā nārācān sūryasaṃnibhānb jagrāha samare pārtho bhūyo bahuśilīmukhānb tais tadānīṃ mahābāhuḥ kṛpasya ratharakṣiṇaḥb jaghāna kṣatriyaśreṣṭhān yudhyamānān mahābalānb candraketuḥ suketuś ca citrāśvo maṇimāṃs tathāb muñjamaulī ca vikrānto hemavarmā bhayāvahaḥb suratho tirathaś caiva suṣeṇo riṣṭa eva cab nṛketuś ca sahānīkās te nipetur gatāsavaḥc tvaran gāṇḍīvanirmuktair arjunas tasya vājinaḥe caturbhiś caturas tīkṣṇair avidhyat parameṣubhiḥa te hayā niśitair viddhā jvaladbhir iva pannagaiḥc utpetuḥ sahasā sarve kṛpaḥ sthānād athācyavata cyutaṃ tu gautamaṃ sthānāt samīkṣya kurunandanaḥc nāvidhyat paravīraghno rakṣamāṇo sya gauravama sa tu labdhvā punaḥ sthānaṃ gautamaḥ savyasācinamc vivyādha daśabhir bāṇais tvaritaḥ kaṅkapatribhiḥa tataḥ pārtho dhanus tasya bhallena niśitena cac cicchedaikena bhūyaś ca hastāc cāpam athāharata athāsya kavacaṃ bāṇair niśitair marmabhedibhiḥc vyadhaman na ca pārtho sya śarīram avapīḍayata tasya nirmucyamānasya kavacāt kāya ābabhauc samaye mucyamānasya sarpasyeva tanur yathāa chinne dhanuṣi pārthena so nyad ādāya kārmukamc cakāra gautamaḥ sajyaṃ tad adbhutam ivābhavata sa tad apy asya kaunteyaś ciccheda nataparvaṇāc evam anyāni cāpāni bahūni kṛtahastavate śāradvatasya ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ paravīrahāa sa chinnadhanur ādāya atha śaktiṃ pratāpavānc prāhiṇot pāṇḍuputrāya pradīptām aśanīm ivad atha śaktiṃ parāmṛśya sūryavaiśvānaraprabhāmd cikṣepa sahasā kruddhaḥ pārthāyādbhutakarmaṇea tām arjunas tadāyāntīṃ śaktiṃ hemavibhūṣitāmc viyadgatāṃ maholkābhāṃ ciccheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥe sāpatad daśadhā chinnā bhūmau pārthena dhīmatāf śaktyāṃ tu vinikṛttāyāṃ virathaḥ śarapīḍitaḥa yugamadhye tu bhallais tu tataḥ sa sadhanuḥ kṛpaḥb pragṛhītvā rathas tūrṇaṃ rathād anyan mahādhanuḥc tam āśu niśitaiḥ pārthaṃ bibheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥa tataḥ pārtho mahātejā viśikhān agnitejasaḥc cikṣepa samare kruddhas trayodaśa śilāśitānd tān nihatya tataḥ pārtho nimeṣād iva bhāratad punar anyān samādatta trayodaśa śilīmukhāna athāsya yugam ekena caturbhiś caturo hayānc ṣaṣṭhena ca śiraḥ kāyāc chareṇa rathasāratheḥa tribhis triveṇuṃ samare dvābhyām akṣau mahābalaḥc dvādaśena tu bhallena cakartāsya dhvajaṃ tathāa tato vajranikāśena phalgunaḥ prahasann ivac trayodaśenendrasamaḥ kṛpaṃ vakṣasy atāḍayata sa chinnadhanvā viratho hatāśvo hatasārathiḥc gadāpāṇir avaplutya tūrṇaṃ cikṣepa tāṃ gadāmc   rathāt tūrṇam amitrahāc gadāṃ cikṣepa sahasā pārthāyāmitatejasea sā tu muktā gadā gurvī kṛpeṇa supariṣkṛtāc arjunena śarair nunnā pratimārgam athāgamatd atha khaḍgaṃ samuddhṛtya śatacandraṃ ca bhānumatd iyeṣa pāṇḍavaṃ hantuṃ kṛpo laghuparākramaḥd sa śaradvatsutas tūrṇaṃ mahācāryaḥ suśikṣitaḥd khecaro vicacāraikaḥ kramāc carmāsidhṛg vibhuḥd tataḥ kṣurāgraiḥ kaunteyo daśabhiḥ khaḍgacarmaṇīd nimeṣād iva ciccheda tad adbhutam ivābhavatd viṣaṇṇavadanas tatra yuddhād apagatodyamaḥd aśvatthāmnas tu sa rathaṃ kṛpaḥ samabhipupluved svasrīyasya mahātejā jagrāha ca dhanuḥ punaḥd tadā gāṇḍīvanirmuktaiḥ khaḍgaṃ tasya nyavārayatd vināśāt khaḍgacarmaṇoḥd dantair dantacchadān daṣṭvā cukopa hṛdi dīrghavatd bhavatv iti punaś coktvāa tato yodhāḥ parīpsantaḥ śāradvatam amarṣaṇamc sarvataḥ samare pārthaṃ śaravarṣair avākirana tato virāṭasya sutaḥ savyam āvṛtya vājinaḥc yamakaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tān yodhān pratyavārayata tataḥ kṛpam upādāya virathaṃ te nararṣabhāḥc apājahrur mahāvegāḥ kuntīputrād dhanaṃjayāt vaiśaṃpāyana uvāca kṛpe panīte droṇas tu pragṛhya sumahad dhanuḥ abhyadravad anādhṛṣyaḥ śoṇāśvaḥ śvetavāhanam sa tu rukmarathaṃ dṛṣṭvā gurum āyāntam antikāt arjuno rathināṃ śreṣṭha uttaraṃ vākyam abravīt arjuna uvācaa yatraiṣā kāñcanī vedī pradīptāgniśikhopamāc ucchritā kāñcane daṇḍe patākābhir alaṃkṛtāe tatra māṃ vaha bhadraṃ te droṇānīkāya māriṣaf bhāradvājena yotsye ham ācāryeṇa mahātmanāf vaiśaṃpāyanaḥf jitaṃ vaikartanaṃ dṛṣṭvā pārtho vairāṭim abravītf sthiro bhava tvaṃ saṃgrāme jayo smākaṃ nṛpātmajaf yāvac chaṅkham upādhmāsye dviṣatāṃ romaharṣaṇamf aviklavam asaṃbhrāntam avyagrahṛdayekṣaṇamf yāhi śīghraṃ yato droṇo mamācāryo mahārathaḥf tathā saṃkrīḍamānasya arjunasya raṇājiref balaṃ sattvaṃ ca tejaś ca lāghavaṃ cāpy avardhataf uttaraḥf tac cādbhutam abhiprekṣya bhayam uttaram āviśatf astrāṇāṃ tava divyānāṃ śaraughān kṣipataś ca tef mano me muhyate tyarthaṃ tava dṛṣṭvā parākramamf dvaidhībhūtaṃ mano mahyaṃ bhayād bharatasattamaf adṛṣṭapūrvaṃ paśyāmi tava gāṇḍīvanisvanamf tava bāhubalaṃ caiva dhanuḥ prākarṣato bahuf vaiśaṃpāyanaḥf tava tejo durādharṣaṃ yathā viṣṇos trivikramef tam uttaraś citram avekṣya gāṇḍivaṃf śarāṃś ca muktān sahasā kirīṭināf bhīto bravīd arjunam ājimadhyef nāhaṃ tavāśvān viṣahe niyantumf tam abravīd īṣad iva prahasyaf gāṇḍīvadhanvā dviṣatāṃ nihantāf mayā sahāyena kuto sti te bhayaṃf praihy uttarāśvān upamantrya vāhayaf āśvāsitas tena dhanaṃjayenaf vairāṭir aśvān pratutoda śīghramf dhanaṃjayaś cāpi nikṛṣya cāpaṃf viṣphārayām āsa mahendrakalpaḥf uttaraṃ caiva bībhatsur abravīt punar arjunaḥf na bhetavyaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ tāta saṃgrāmamūrdhanif rājaputro si bhadraṃ te kule mahati mātsyakef jātas tvaṃ kṣatriyakule na viṣīditum arhasif dhṛtiṃ kṛtvā suvipulāṃ rājaputra rathaṃ mamaf yudhyamānasya samare śatrubhiḥ saha vāhayaf uktvā tam evaṃ bībhatsur arjunaḥ punar abravītf pāṇḍavo rathināṃ śreṣṭho bhāradvājaṃ samīkṣya tua aśvāḥ śoṇāḥ prakāśante bṛhantaś cāruvāhinaḥc snigdhavidrumasaṃkāśās tāmrāsyāḥ priyadarśanāḥe yuktā rathavare yasya sarvaśikṣāviśāradāḥf yatto rathavare śūraḥ sarvaśastrabhṛtāṃ varaḥa dīrghabāhur mahātejā balarūpasamanvitaḥc sarvalokeṣu vikhyāto bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavāna buddhyā tulyo hy uśanasā bṛhaspatisamo nayec vedās tathaiva catvāro brahmacaryaṃ tathaiva caa sasaṃhārāṇi divyāni sarvāṇy astrāṇi māriṣac dhanurvedaś ca kārtsnyena yasmin
